Foreign Telegrams

Japanese Bandits Run Rampant 54

Disaster Strikes from Heaven

Earthquake Strikes Tokyo Area

Small Citizens and Livestock Suffer

Reuters, Tokyo, 21st - At 11:20 AM this morning, a rather severe earthquake struck Tokyo. The people were terrified and frantically ran out of their houses. There was considerable damage, but it was limited to collapsing walls and broken windows. Several fires broke out but were quickly extinguished. Telephone and telegraph communications were disrupted, so the situation elsewhere is unknown. Damage in Yokohama was similar to Tokyo, with some walls collapsing and several chimneys destroyed. There were few casualties.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 21st - Tokyo City and its vicinity experienced an earthquake this morning. The most severe damage occurred in Kitada Village, within the jurisdiction of the Hongchao Police Station in Saitama Prefecture, where an elementary school collapsed during class, causing numerous deaths and injuries to children. Many other schools and residences collapsed, and a considerable number of people and livestock were also injured. In Tokyo City, telephone lines were cut in 23 places, and power lines were also cut. Many walls collapsed, and all the water in the indoor containers was spilled. The epicenter seems to be near Tokyo, but the damage near the epicenter is not significant. According to reports from various places, the Jōetsu Line's Isobuchi Tunnel and the first Apt-style tunnel of the Yuzawa Tunnel collapsed, causing trains on the line to be unable to move forward or backward. Sendai City also experienced a considerable strong earthquake. The time felt by the human body in Numazu was very short. The maximum amplitude in Saitama was 25 meters, with the most severe damage. The amplitude in Nagoya was 22 meters, with no apparent damage. Osaka experienced only a weak earthquake. According to the Central Meteorological Observatory, the maximum amplitude reached 55 meters, and the epicenter seemed to be near the Sengenyama area in the upper reaches of the Arakawa River.

England 55

Financial Turmoil

Government Temporarily Responds to Emergency

Announces Suspension of Gold Standard

To Prevent Continued Outflow of Cash

To Prevent Continued Outflow of Cash

World Stock Exchanges Suspend Trading

Japan Particularly Panicked

Reuters, London, 21st – Britain has now suspended the gold standard. Last night, the government issued a statement saying that after consultation with the Bank of England, it has been decided that the clause in the 1925 Gold Standard Act that allows the Bank of England to sell cash at a fixed price must be suspended. This bill has now been submitted to the Lower House, with the aim of passing it through both houses today. Although the bill has not yet passed, the Bank of England has been ordered to begin implementation, which it has been doing since midnight. At the same time, the Bank of England announced that the discount rate would be increased from 4.5% to 6% from this morning. In recent months, cash has been flowing out of the London market continuously, and the government has been forced to take this measure. Yesterday's sharp drop in the price of British gold in New York caused Prime Minister MacDonald to rush back to London from his country villa to consult with Bank of England officials and convene a special cabinet meeting. After the meeting, this statement was issued. The UK resumed the gold standard in April 1925, and overseas autonomous states soon followed suit. By the end of the following year, countries using gold as currency accounted for 60% of the world's population. The so-called gold standard, briefly speaking, means that currency can be legally exchanged for a fixed amount of cash. All currency obligations must be met with cash at a fixed rate. Therefore, in countries that implement the gold standard, the exchange rate of their currency with foreign countries is linked to the price of gold, and their exchange rate with other gold standard countries varies depending on whether it is more profitable to import or export cash. The British government's move can slightly eliminate the reasons for manipulating the British currency. From now on, the price of the British currency will not be linked to gold, but to international debt. In other words, it depends on whether foreign creditor countries can or are willing to maintain the stability of the British currency. Paris has expressed that the French Ministry of Finance is eager to provide the necessary funds to protect the British currency from fluctuations. Since mid-July, the cash, foreign currency, and debt withdrawn from the London market have totaled £200 million. In recent days, the Netherlands and other countries have withdrawn a significant amount of foreign currency from the UK, so the British government has a real need to protect the Bank of England's gold reserves. This decision does not affect the British government's and the Bank of England's obligation to pay debts in foreign currency. The Bank of England's gold reserves currently total £130 million, which is sufficient to meet various emergency needs, but it is felt that at the current time, it is not appropriate to further reduce gold reserves by allowing European countries to withdraw them. European withdrawals are based on psychological factors, namely a sudden lack of confidence in the UK's financial capabilities. The London Stock Exchange is closed today, but the settlement of transactions is still ongoing. Ordinary banking business will not be suspended and will remain open as usual. There is no reason for British currency transactions to be affected, but banks have agreed to cooperate and restrict Britons from buying foreign currency. However, those needed for commercial purposes or to fulfill existing contracts are not subject to these restrictions. The government has also issued a warning, saying that while it does not believe that the current difficulties are entirely due to the outflow of funds by Britons, most of the withdrawals are due to foreigners. However, the government is willing to reiterate the warning issued by the Financial Secretary in the Lower House: any Briton who buys foreign currency himself or helps others to do so, thereby increasing the tension in the foreign exchange market, is deliberately aggravating the country's difficulties. It is also said that the country's wealth is great, and the government is confident that the current exchange difficulties are only temporary. The decision to suspend the gold standard was made by the entire cabinet. The Bank of England had hoped to avoid this move, but the large-scale withdrawals on Friday and Saturday prompted an urgent plan to be implemented immediately. It is generally speculated that the suspension of the gold standard will last for seven months. British newspapers all welcomed this move, and even the opposition Labour Party's newspaper called it appropriate.

Reuters, London, 21st – This afternoon, the Prime Minister formally submitted the 1931 Gold Standard Act to the Lower House. Financial Secretary Snowden will issue a statement to explain the bill and will second it. It is expected that there will be no opposition in the Lower House. After the Lower House passes it, it will be submitted to the specially convened Upper House, and then, with the approval of the King, it will take effect tonight. It is reported that the bill contains three main clauses: (1) Suspending part of the 1925 Gold Standard Act; (2) Compensating the Bank of England for the losses caused by the cabinet's orders; (3) Stipulating regulations (if necessary, by order of the Treasury) to deal with any situation that has occurred or may occur. The last clause is expected to be aimed at any amount of British capital flowing abroad. If grain prices soar, the government will immediately stop it. The bill is valid for six months, but it can be extended through ordinary parliamentary procedures. The election issue has been put aside because of yesterday's government decision. Reuters, London, 21st – This morning, people rubbed their eyes and were stunned when they read the newspaper reports about the government's measures yesterday. It was unexpected and they did not understand its meaning. Most people do not understand the complicated issues of the gold standard, so they questioned each other. On the trains to the city, there was also a lot of talk about this matter. All kinds of workers seemed deeply concerned and eager to know how the government's decision would affect them. Merchants and securities brokers were also shocked after reading the newspapers. The streets leading to the stock exchange, which are usually very lively around 10 o'clock, were almost deserted today because the government ordered the market to be closed. It is generally believed that the reason for the suspension is to prevent foreign countries from selling British securities on a large scale. On Saturday and Sunday, the stock exchange was open all day, and foreigners who held British securities sold them off, causing prices to fall.

Reuters, Paris, 21st – Newspapers of all parties praised the courage of the British people in dealing with the financial crisis. Le Matin reported that the French government is now quickly considering the plans to be taken. Minister of Finance Flandin convened a meeting of experts this morning to receive the best advice on the issue. Several experts have rushed back from Geneva. The Banque de France currently has 12,500,000,000 francs in London.

Reuters, Paris, 21st – After consulting with Minister of Finance Flandin, French Prime Minister Laval declared that the French government is closely monitoring the situation in the UK and is willing to assist the British government.

Reuters, London, 21st – Today, large silver bars soared. The near-term rose nearly two pence, from 12 pence and 15/16ths the day before to 14 pence and 3/8ths today. The forward rose one and a half pence, from 13 pence the day before to 14 and a half pence today.

Reuters, London, 21st – European stock exchanges are almost all closed today.

Reuters, Calcutta, 21st – The stock exchanges here and in Bombay were not open today.

Reuters, Copenhagen, 21st – Due to the UK's suspension of part of the gold standard, the Copenhagen Stock Exchange decided to suspend trading today.

Reuters, Berlin, 21st – The board of directors of the Berlin Stock Exchange met this morning to discuss the measures to be taken after the UK suspended part of the gold standard. A director told a Reuters reporter that the Berlin Stock Exchange must be temporarily closed. It is rumored that the German government will adopt more stringent plans to restrict foreign exchange transactions. It is heard that the national bank will raise the discount rate.

Reuters, New York, 21st – New York banking circles said that the British government's suspension of the gold standard is a constructive measure prompted by a temporary emergency. The loans recently borrowed by the US Federal Reserve Bank and Morgan Company to the UK are stipulated to be repaid in US dollars, so they are not affected. There is also no relationship with the US dollar debt issued by the UK in the US. It is expected that British banking officials will follow the German method of managing foreign exchange. When the news of the British government's decision reached here, securities brokers were quite shaken, but important bankers said that this matter has very little impact on the US because the US has far fewer short-term funds deposited in London than in Berlin, estimated at no more than $50 million.

Reuters, Tokyo, 21st – The Tokyo Stock Exchange panicked upon hearing the news of the UK's suspension of the gold standard and immediately suspended trading. Although the Osaka Stock Exchange did not suspend trading immediately, prices fell sharply and it also suspended trading soon after. The Minister of Finance claimed that Japan and other countries may be indirectly affected, but Japan does not need to restore the gold embargo. After the war, Japan's gold accounts have been transferred from London to the United States, so he expects that Japanese finances can avoid direct impact.

Central Government Holds 56

Memorial Service for Zhu Zhixin's Martyrdom

Dai Chuanxian Speaks on Japan's Disregard for Justice and Exploitation of Danger

Those Who Are Disloyal, Unfilial, Unbenevolent, and Unrighteous Have No Reason to Exist

At 9 a.m. on the 21st, the Central Party Headquarters held a memorial service for the 11th anniversary of Zhu Zhixin's martyrdom and the 130th memorial week. Central Committee members Kong Xiangxi, Zhang Daofan, Shao Lizi, Fang Juehui, Dai Chuanxian, Ding Weifen, Wu Jingheng, Zhang Renjie, Chen Lifu, and Shao Yuanchong, as well as staff and guests, totaling more than 600 people, attended. Dai Chuanxian presided over the meeting. After paying respects, Dai made the following report: "Comrades, today is the 11th anniversary of Mr. Zhu Zhixin's martyrdom. This year, as we commemorate Mr. Zhu, our country is suffering from severe natural and man-made disasters, and has also been subjected to major foreign trampling. We should make a unanimous and painful determination to learn from Mr. Zhu's character and from the Prime Minister's character. All party comrades and all the people of the country should take Mr. Zhu's ambition as their own and the Prime Minister's heart as their own, abandon all personal opinions, emotions, and interests, and unite sincerely to save the country from danger. This time, Japan suddenly sent troops to the three northeastern provinces, occupying Changchun in the north, Yingkou in the west, and Andong in the south in one day and night. At the same time, it increased its troops in Qingdao and took action towards Jinzhou. All the places in the east, west, south, and north of Liaoning Province were occupied by the Japanese army. Hebei and Shandong were also under threat at the same time. All the arsenals, important administrative organs, industrial organs, cultural organs, and financial organs in Liaoning were occupied. There is no precedent for such a barbaric and tyrannical country in the world. There is no precedent for such a barbaric and tyrannical act in the world. Human civilization exists for the survival and happiness of mankind, so civilization is justice, and justice is civilization. China has thousands of years of civilization and thousands of years of education. No matter how deep the personal grudges are between individuals, if others are in great danger, they must not be treated cruelly and violently. The same is true for countries. Therefore, since ancient times, China's national morality has advocated continuing what has been cut off, raising what has been abolished, governing chaos and maintaining danger, rescuing disasters and comforting difficulties, and being generous in giving and frugal in taking. China has been the largest country in Asia for thousands of years, and has never destroyed other countries or invaded their lands. Moreover, it has only helped neighboring countries in times of disaster and danger, and has never taken the opportunity to plunder. This time, China's flood is an unprecedented disaster since the ancient floods. The disaster area covers sixteen provinces, and the number of victims is close to 100 million. The three rivers and two rivers are full of collapsed cities and destroyed ponds, and there are corpses everywhere. There are displaced people everywhere. In this situation, Japan, a neighboring country of the same race and culture that has been influenced by Chinese culture for thousands of years, does not provide relief, but instead takes the opportunity to plunder, sending troops to occupy our territory, destroy our treasuries, and kill our people. Such a cruel and inhuman country is not as good as a poisonous cannibalistic race. It can be said that it is a disgrace to mankind and a humiliation to civilization. Recalling nine years ago, Japan also suffered a strange disaster of a major earthquake. At that time, how did the countries of the world express their sympathy and provide all kinds of assistance? All of Japan's requests were unconditionally granted by all countries, and the voluntary requests for relief were too numerous to remember. Therefore, it has today's revival. Looking only at Germany, after the European war, it suffered a major blow and its economy was extremely difficult. Its relief to Japan was also all-encompassing and sincere. Valuable books in the library, as long as there were two copies, were willing to give one to him. Therefore, the world treats him like that for his cultural recovery today. He treats his neighboring countries like this. Moreover, China is of the same race and is the motherland of his civilization. Everything he eats, wears, lives, travels, writes, speaks, and has cultural relics and institutions, which one is not a grace from China? Such ingratitude and opportunistic robbery is truly heartbreaking. We are convinced that such a disloyal, unfilial, unbenevolent, and unrighteous thing has no reason to exist if the world's justice is not destroyed. Today, as we commemorate Mr. Zhu, we hope that all party comrades and all the people of the country will be thoroughly awakened, regardless of north, south, east, or west, old or young, male or female, to be sincere and sincere, abandon all disputes of emotion and disputes of interest, and unite to learn from the Prime Minister and Mr. Zhu's love for the country, love for the people, love for comrades, and love for justice, and fight to the end with the determination to die."

Students of the East Asian Tongwen Academy Boycott Classes

The East Asian Tongwen Academy in Xujiahui, this municipality, is an aggressive machine established by Japanese imperialism under the guise of scholarship. It has been in operation for 31 years. After graduating in four years, they are introduced by the school authorities to serve in Japanese agencies in Northeast China, acting as pioneers for Japanese imperialism's aggression against our country. However, Japanese imperialism has never shed its ferocious face towards our country. Municipal Education Bureau Orders Two Women's Physical Education Schools to Change Names 60

World Education Association 61

Guo Bingwen Reelected as Vice President

The World Education Association held its Fourth General Assembly from July 28th to August 2nd of this year in Denver, Colorado, USA. We have received a report from the association stating that the assembly was attended by representatives from 29 countries, totaling over 3,800 people. Many resolutions were passed, the most important of which were: (1) to develop health education; (2) to promote the improvement of rural education; (3) to cultivate teachers suitable for the times; (4) to promote international understanding through educational methods; (5) to jointly seek the popularization of education and reduce the number of illiterate people; (6) to fully utilize films and wireless telephones to aid the progress of education; (7) to suggest that governments of various countries establish educational counselors in major embassies, etc. Furthermore, the officers were re-elected, with Dr. Monroe of the United States elected as President, Mr. Hans Hensen of England elected as Vice President for the European region, Mr. Hu Qiaoshi of Canada elected as Vice President for the American region, and Dr. Guo Bingwen of China elected as Vice President for the Asian region. Jiangsu Provincial Preliminary Rounds for the National Games - Day One 67

Zhuang Mingzhen Breaks National Women's Long Jump Record | 4.55 Meters

Zhenjiang Correspondent reports that the Jiangsu Provincial Preliminary Rounds for the National Games are aimed at training athletes.

The first day dawned with clear skies and bright autumn sunshine. The reporter arrived at the venue at 8 AM and found athletes gathering on the field, practicing freely. The rostrum was quiet as the meeting time had not yet arrived. After some time, guests and organizers arrived one after another. The meeting began at 9 AM. All athletes marched around the field, flags flying, showing great vitality. After the music played, formalities were observed.

Chairman Chen Hexian said in his speech that today's Jiangsu preliminary round is taking place while the country is suffering from widespread floods. The central government has decided to temporarily suspend all activities, except for the National Games, which will proceed as planned. We must understand that sports are related to the survival of the nation and the people, which is different from ordinary matters. The purpose of our participation in sports is not only to break records and win championships, but also to emphasize the importance of a healthy body and a healthy mind for any endeavor. The work of struggle cannot be achieved merely by propaganda or issuing a declaration or writing an article. For example, today we all know that the Japanese have unjustifiably occupied Shenyang in our Northeast, massacring our people. Our people have only retreated, unprepared. The people's cultivation is also unsound. It is a shame to be insulted by neighboring countries in this way. If we want to fight the enemy at this time, we must rely on the people having a healthy physique to win. Today, everyone is participating in the preliminary round under such painful circumstances, and we must have a deep understanding of this point. Finished. Next,

Yu Qingtang reported the number of counties and people participating in the sports meet. There were 18 counties, 254 male participants, and 76 female participants. There were 19 school units and 18 public units. In addition to track and field events, there were 1 male volleyball team, 1 male football team, 8 male basketball teams, and 9 male tennis teams. In addition to track and field events, there were 3 female volleyball teams, 2 female basketball teams, and 1 female tennis team. In addition, there was also a heartfelt expression of grief over the Japanese occupation of Shenyang in the three northeastern provinces. The representative of the Provincial Party Department, Lan Weibin, gave a training speech, stating that Japan has no way out for its surplus population each year. Going south, the South Seas Islands have been almost completely developed by various countries. Going north, it is ice and snow, which cannot be used. Only our country has a pleasant climate and fertile land, which is enough to fulfill its continental dream, not hesitating to defy the world. We did not start a war without reason. You are all young people with blood. If you don’t have a healthy physique, how can you take on the important responsibilities in the future? Your attendance at this meeting is not for personal face, not for a school’s honor, but for the survival of the country. (1) Track and Field Competition

Free Talk

Chatting by the Court Grass Studio

The Pen That Does Not Turn 68

Many of my peers have become officials, and some are even high-ranking officials. Some of them are doing quite well, while others are somewhat muddled on major issues but clear on minor ones. I wrote a poem to advise them to be mindful of Dong Hu's resurrection. But there are so many officials in the world, and the muddled ones are not limited to my friends. Now I am willing to offer this poem to friends to all officials in the world. Let’s all work hard!

"Do not be a muddled official…

Ten thousand people in sorrow, one person in joy.

Dong Hu has a pen harder than iron,

Writing only right and wrong, never turning."

World Tidbits 69

— Sea Guest

Treasures on the Beach: There are several beaches along the coast of England where one can find a large number of gemstones. Although not rare treasures, agates and topaz are not ordinary items either. Yet they are often found on the beach, allowing people to gain without labor. Recently, the Bishop of Plymouth dedicated a set of altar lamps to St. Andrews Church, inlaid with forty-eight beautiful topaz stones. It is said that all of them were picked up from the beach by a female parishioner. She initially only picked up forty stones and gave them to the lamp maker, asking if they could be used. The lamp maker first drew a pattern, but found that the forty stones were not enough to distribute and that eight more were needed. The female parishioner, hearing this, hurried back to the beach and searched for a week, finally fulfilling her wish.

Scarlet amber can often be found on the beaches along the east coast of England. It is said to have washed up all the way from the Baltic Sea. Near the mouths of several large rivers in Scotland, many pearl divers collect pearls from shells. They obtain a lot, and the pearls are large and beautiful, welcomed by women, thus gaining great profit.

What I Saw on Wusong Road, Hongkou, on the Morning of September 19, 1931 70

— Wang Mingxin

Recently, Sino-Japanese negotiations have become increasingly tense. Japanese soldiers are openly advocating for a military solution, showing their disregard for China and international justice. Although our country has been pursuing a policy of peace and making concessions, the Japanese have been unrelenting in their demands. The voice of preparation for war is becoming increasingly urgent. Those with insight have long expected that there would be no good outcome. Now, they blatantly disregard public opinion and violently occupied the provincial capital of Liaoning on the evening of the 18th at 10:30 PM. They are further expanding their ambitions and have begun shelling our national army in various places along the South Manchurian Railway. It is clear that this was organized and prepared in advance. The cause of the conflict and how our authorities are responding will not be discussed here. What follows is a description of the actions of the Japanese on Wusong Road on the 19th. I wonder what our compatriots will think after reading this.

Japanese telegraph propaganda is known for its speed. As the conflict broke out, most Chinese people were still dreaming, but the Japanese Daily News on Wusong Road posted a war report next to its gate at 5 AM and issued special editions. By 11 AM, there were seven telegrams posted. The large-character headline read "Major Sino-Japanese Military Conflict." At 10:30 PM on the 18th, the attack on Beida Camp began (the residence of the Northeast Army, magnificently built on a national scale, capable of accommodating 200,000 people). By 1:30 AM on the 19th, it was completely occupied. At 3 AM, the commercial district was cleared, and at 6:30 AM, the city of Liaoning was completely occupied. All Chinese military police were disarmed, and so on. At the same time, major Japanese stores on Wusong Road distributed the same war reports and posted them outside their doors. Being in the middle of it felt like being on a battlefield. Chinese people who saw it were indignant, while the Japanese showed smiles and were arrogant. The tension in everyone's hearts was high, and there was a possibility of conflict at any time. However, once one crossed Wusong Road to Great Horse Road and Fuzhou Road, the scene was bustling and peaceful, as usual. This shows the numbness of the Chinese people. Unable to calm down after returning home, I especially record this to inform my compatriots, hoping they will wake up quickly.

A Day at Ye Garden 71

— Tang Hua

Since the opening of Ye Garden in Jiangwan, I have long wanted to visit, but I have been unable to do so due to busy schedules. The 19th was the first day of the charity performance for flood relief in various provinces held in the garden, so I made time to visit. Upon arrival, the scene was bustling and prosperous, crowded with tourists, all enthusiastic men and women, which is admirable. It was the most grand occasion ever seen on Jiangwan Road. The following is a brief description of the highlights of the event.

Because I was new to Ye Garden, I was unfamiliar with the paths. Fortunately, upon entering, Boy Scouts distributed maps, allowing me to explore everything. The garden is full of layered hills and greenery, a unique paradise. The best views are Fuhu Ridge, Qianlong Pool, Purple Bamboo Forest, Little Tiantai, Willow Waves Listening to Orioles, and Odd Peaks Inserting Clouds. Other places such as Little Luofu, Glazed Pavilion, Qingtang Bridge, and Lakeside Pavilion are also fascinating, as if one were in a fairyland.

This time, because a 49-foot-high Temple of Heaven was built in the garden, the 63rd generation Zhang Tianshi from Longhu Mountain in Jiangxi was specially invited to chase and sacrifice the souls of the disaster victims. Most tourists wanted to catch a glimpse of Tianshi's true face, and his appeal can be described as great. The Temple of Heaven was made of bamboo and wood and surrounded by yellow cloth, towering above the clouds. Eight trigram flags were hung above, fluttering in the air. In the evening, the electric lights were all lit up, as bright as day. The perimeter of the garden was hung with lanterns of various colors, adding to the splendor. There were countless entertainment programs. As far as I know, the Yongyi Film Company's entire cast performed the drama "Disaster Tragedy." The plot was sad and moving. The performances of Li Changjian and the two ladies Li Li and Wang Guiqiu were particularly tearful and energetic. At that time, a gentleman in the audience threw silver coins onto the stage five times, making a clanging sound. So one person responded to a hundred calls and took out money one after another. Then, the person in charge and a tourist served as witnesses and put the money into the donation box. From this, we can know the depth of the drama's appeal. After the performance, the manager of the company, Zhao Yongni, performed head-hitting iron, which was thrilling and breathtaking.

Guan Shengyuan specially sold noodles and dim sum in the garden. According to what Xi Guansheng told me, some of the proceeds will be used to help with disaster relief. I also met Qian Huafo, one of the initiators of the event, who has been abandoning painting and arranging the venue for days. According to him, the event will last for a total of five days, with entertainment programs changing every day. Fireworks and river lanterns will be lit in the evening. (Move and reward for disaster relief)

A Discussion of the Lives of Gandhi and Tagore 72

— Yunshan

(1)

Mr. Jingwan convened a "Lunch Talk." Those attending were prominent, although not necessarily the elite of the nation, but they came from all directions, which was also rare. Among them were Ms. Hu Lanqi, who had recently returned to China with Madam Sun; Ms. Lu Jingqing, who had returned from Japan; Ms. Tao Xuan, a female member of the Legislative Yuan who came to Shanghai from Beijing yesterday; and Mr. Zhou Shoujuan and Mr. Huang Jiping, both reporters from Shenbao. I had returned from Tibet and India a month ago. Jingwan asked Ms. Hu to talk about Madam Sun's life, and instructed me to talk about the lives of Gandhi and Tagore. After the talks, Mr. Zhou was ordered to take notes to fill the "Free Talk" column. This is not writing a formal essay, but merely providing some conversation material.

(2)

The Chinese people have seen many photos of Mr. Gandhi, with his skinny frame, bare body, bald head, and bare feet. His "thinness" surpasses that of Mr. Shoujuan; there is no comparison. From his photos with his skinny frame, bare body, bald head, and bare feet, one can imagine his life.

Mr. Gandhi was originally the son of a wealthy family, but now he has no property or home. His wife and children follow him, constantly moving, never settling down, to engage in national revolution and the transformation of the country and society. His clothing is all spun and woven by himself, and little sewing is involved. In the summer, he only wears a cloth around his lower body. In the cold, he puts on a shawl over his upper body. Wherever he goes, he carries a spinning wheel with him. Indians who come to see him all wear "Gandhi cloth," and no one wears a Western suit or foreign clothes. Even Westerners who come to see him do the same. His diet is simple and light, mainly consisting of goat's milk and vegetables. He absolutely forbids killing animals and eating meat.

He usually gets up at four in the morning. His bedding is a wooden bed and a straw mat, or he sleeps directly on the ground. After washing and bathing, he holds a morning meeting with his disciples, reciting poems, singing songs, and engaging in silent prayer. During the day, in addition to working and meeting guests, he often spins yarn, reads books, and writes articles. He takes walks outside the village around six in the morning and evening. He remains silent one day each week, not uttering a sound, to rest. If there is something to say, he communicates with writing or gestures. This day is called "Silence Day." However, work such as spinning yarn, reading books, writing articles, and clearing correspondence continues as usual. In short, Mr. Gandhi's life can be summarized as "austere." Mr. Gandhi was born in 1869 and is sixty-two years old this year.

(3)

Mr. Tagore is known to the world as a poet and philosopher. But Mr. Tagore is not only a poet and philosopher, but also a musician and painter. In other words, he is a complete artistic poet and philosopher. And Mr. Tagore's life is also an artistic poetic and philosophical life. Mr. Tagore's family is even more noble than that of Mr. Gandhi. His grandfather and father were both saints of India. Mr. Tagore has further advanced and glorified their legacy. Mr. Tagore's old home is in Calcutta, but he often resides in his newly built private property at Santiniketan International University. The architecture is beautiful, exquisite, and also very grand, shaped like coral. I once wrote four lines of poetry to praise it:

"A coral-shaped building,

This is the poet's home.

I hope the poet sings,

And chants more about slums."

Mr. Tagore's clothing and food are also very frugal. Although he does not spin and weave himself like Gandhi, all his clothes are Indian products. He regards Western suits and foreign clothes as shameful. His food mainly consists of milk, sweets, and vegetables, but he does not abstain from meat. He gets up early at four in the morning to pray for world peace and happiness. He takes outdoor walks before sunrise, three seasons a year (Indian weather is divided into three seasons), regardless of the heat or cold. During the day, in addition to reading books and writing poems, he often writes articles and paints. His hand never stops writing or painting. He even places books beside him during meals. In the evening, he summons male and female students to sing the poems and songs he has composed. The sound overflows, filling the ears. When he completes a new article, he immediately gives a lecture, his voice clear and loud like a bell. He usually receives guests after four in the afternoon. In spring and winter, famous people from Europe and America come from thousands of miles away to catch a glimpse of Mr. Tagore's demeanor, in an endless stream.

Mr. Tagore was born in 1861 and is exactly seventy years old this year. In summary, Mr. Tagore's life can be described as "happy."

(4)

Having briefly discussed the lives of Mr. Gandhi and Mr. Tagore, I would like to add one more word. We are born into this Saha world, and we should wish that everyone's life is like Tagore's, but for our own temporary life, we should learn from Gandhi.

Rotary Club

A Husband's Wife (20) 73

— Jiang Hongjiao

Mr. Chen's heart was pounding, his breathing was unusually heavy, much more so than usual. The teacup in his hand was trembling. Besides Madam Li, he saw nothing in front of him, like being slightly drunk from overindulging in alcohol, in a daze. He didn't understand what was happening. He was even more confused, wondering if he was a married man, and if she was a married woman. Was this situation reasonable? He only felt that her beauty, her tenderness, her pity, her temperament, and her will all suited him. Her not rejecting his attentiveness was a precious thing. He felt that only she was his confidante, and decided to treat her as an ideal lover or wife.

"Have you found out about the matter I entrusted to you?" Madam Li spoke first, after a long silence between the two.

"I am very sorry, I haven't inquired about it yet. But I think it's best for you not to know about this matter. Knowing it will only cause you more trouble. Haven't I advised you repeatedly?" Mr. Chen sat beside her. She turned to the side, making room for him to sit down. Their bodies were now very close.

"I consider myself a woman, and my capacity is not as great as you men. I don't believe that there is any woman in the world who would not inquire about her husband's love history with other women. The woman in the car the other day must have been his lover, without a doubt."

"My wife has been going out with him often these days, maybe she can find out something."

"If you don't want to help me, that's fine; why do you always say this to me? To be honest, I don't really approve of your wife going to the movies and dance halls with my husband."

"Do you suspect that there is something ambiguous between them as well?"

"If you were a woman, and your husband and his friend's wife were so close, would you not be suspicious?"

"Then, starting tomorrow, I will forbid her from associating with Mr. Li again. Would that satisfy you?"

"That's not what I'm aiming for. I've heard people say that one's own writing is the best, and someone else's wife is the best. This can represent the psychology of most men. Do you agree?"

"It's difficult for me to answer this question immediately. I only feel that the union of husband and wife involves more emotion in the beginning. After the initial period, both parties bear a kind of obligation, and the emotion decreases. This is also a very common fact. Because the exchange of emotion is a kind of sacrifice, while obligation is a business matter, with some bargaining and weighing. If there is a slight difference in quality, disputes or resentment will arise. Before I got married, I only imagined that the life of a couple living together would be completely sweet and cooperative. After getting married, I realized that the relationship between husband and wife is such a troublesome thing. So, I think that if men and women have feelings and fall in love, they don't need to get married. It's better to maintain a friendship forever, so that there are no obligations. Without obligations, there will be less trouble, and both will be free."

Commercial News and Finance

Gold Price Plummets 74

A Drastic Drop of Sixty Taels and Six Mace

Rumor of British Ban on Cash Exports: Yesterday, the 21st, the plunge in gold prices was unprecedented, with fluctuations of ten taels in an instant. Each transaction saw swings of at least five mace to one tael. The violent waves were ultimately uncontrollable. From morning to night, there was a difference of about fifty taels. The final disastrous fall of sixty taels was an unexpected and sudden change. This was due to Japan's aggressive actions in the Eastern Provinces, making the situation even more urgent, like a bolt from the blue. Dealers engaged in mass selling, trying to dispose of their holdings, which was severely impacted, creating great fear. The market opened with a sharp drop, and because the silver market rose, sellers did not stop. Short sellers aggressively added to their positions, causing the foreign exchange to weaken. As a result, the gold price broke through 730 taels. The market remained weak, sellers were bold, and exchange rates hardened. British gold at 1425 was difficult to sell, and rumors spread that Britain had banned the export of cash, making people even more fearful. There was a sudden sense of collapse, breaking through the 700 tael mark. Afterwards, buyers appeared, and the market eased, rising by more than ten taels. Later, it fluctuated around 705-6 taels, but the situation was extremely chaotic. Clearing houses were especially chaotic, making it difficult to gather information.

The market opened with a direct plunge. The November opening fell sharply by 24 taels and 6 mace, to 742 taels (although there were fluctuations of over 20 taels within the first ten minutes or so, from 50 taels to within 30 taels). Then, the Dalian group tried to cover their short positions, briefly reaching 47 taels and a half. However, sellers continued to emerge, causing a sharp drop of 16-17 taels, reaching only 31 taels. British gold also eased, with banks trading at 13 and a half. Soon after, November contracts settled at 6875. Before long, it rose by 6 jiao, reaching 37 taels. Unexpectedly, speculators sold heavily, with Bingxing dumping, and Yuankangxiang vying to sell. In an instant, it plummeted by 15 taels, with no turning back. By 9:30, it was at 22 taels. When British gold opened, it was at 28 taels and a half. Drastic Changes in the Silver Dollar Market 77

Impacted by Foreign Aggression... Public Panic Rises Greatly

Dollar Interest Rates Suddenly Soar... Silver Drafts and Clearing Fees Surge

The Market's Chaotic Situation: Yesterday morning, the market situation was still flat and uneventful. The market prices of silver dollars and silver bullion showed no movement. Unexpectedly, drastic changes occurred in the afternoon. Silver interest rates became very tight, exceeding the equilibrium line. Dollar interest rates also showed wild movement. According to inquiries, the changes were due to the impact of foreign aggression, causing public panic. Banks, for the sake of self-defense, tightened their silver interest rates. The commercial prospects of the northern groups were a hidden concern, and there was a possibility that action had to be taken. Therefore, silver drafts and clearing fees rose to new highs not seen this year. As for the changes in dollar interest rates, the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications originally intended to purchase a large number of exchange heads, amounting to two or three million. Seeing that the market atmosphere was not good, with weak selling and very active buyers, it was difficult to close the market for a while. As a result, the closing was extended by three quarters of an hour, starting at 2:15. The Bank of China and the Bank of Communications, seeing that the situation was not good, stopped buying and strongly suppressed the market, preventing it from rising. Therefore, the dollar interest rate only rose by one cent. However, based on overall observations, the situation was not good, and it was feared that tightening would continue today and tomorrow.

Securities Due to Japanese Occupation of Our Southern Manchuria

Unprecedented Plunge in the Securities Market 78

Trading Halted at the Start of the Morning Due to a Sharp Decline

Afternoon Resumption Delayed

Significant Over-the-Counter Trading

Yesterday (21st), the bond market of the local Chinese Securities Exchange was extremely tense. Generally, people felt very uneasy. The Japanese had abandoned the rhetoric of peaceful coexistence and carried out a large-scale invasion, rapidly increasing their troops in the Northeast. They seized the important cities from Southern Manchuria to Qinhuangdao and all the border areas, seizing control and plundering everything, destroying all construction. The impact was unimaginable, causing widespread anxiety and fear in the market. The securities market experienced an unprecedented plunge. At the start of the morning, bonds experienced a surge of selling, universally plummeting, and repeatedly reaching the price limit and halting trading. At the opening, the trading of the current-month futures and demobilization 6, customs 19, customs 20, rolling tobacco tax, consolidated tax, salt tax, and disarmament 19 goodness September futures were all halted. In the next trading period, customs 9 also halted trading. Of those not previously halted, only disarmament 19 goodness October futures and 96 remained. In the afternoon, trading was delayed due to the collection of temporary additional security deposits. Brokers traded over-the-counter, but with no formal market, the over-the-counter prices trended towards stability. The attitude of the financial industry was good, buying some to maintain the market. A few large accounts also invested occasionally. Thus, other than a nearly one-yuan drop in the over-the-counter salt tax, others fluctuated by about half a yuan from the halted price. The market situation was somewhat stable. In addition, in the afternoon, news of a sudden earthquake in Japan, which caused a steep fall in the gold market, which was true, provided some comfort. At about 6 p.m., the market resumed, and the over-the-counter trading was firmer. At the opening, disarmament rose nearly one yuan, disarmament 19 goodness October futures rose by one yuan several jiao from the morning, and 96 also rose significantly. The market trend was still showing a continuous decline. Although the bond market seemed to have a slightly better turn, the future was still uncertain. There were no spot trades yesterday, but the total futures traded was more than 24.7 million yuan, including more than 10 million yuan in over-the-counter settlement and transfer trades. In the afternoon, actual trades of four types totaled only over one million yuan.

Cotton Market Plunges Sharply 80

The cotton market experienced a sharp decline, seemingly beyond control. This was mainly due to the continuous fall in American cotton prices for nine consecutive days, while local market prices remained stagnant. Unexpectedly, gold prices plummeted, and American cotton prices further declined. As a result, the cost of imported cotton became significantly cheaper, and foreign firms offered particularly accommodating prices. Marked Flour Trading Active, Market Weak 84

Yesterday's flour market experienced significant fluctuations after opening in the morning. The opening prices were low, due to a reported decrease of 45 cents to 1-20 cents in imported wheat, and a sharp drop in gold prices of 20-30 taels due to the invasion of the eastern neighbor. This was expected to create a trend. As a result, the opening price for the current month was as low as 2 taels and 5 cents. However, short covering was very active, and some people believed that if war broke out between China and Japan, all the already purchased foreign wheat would have problems. Therefore, there were many who temporarily bought in, and the market turned from weakness to strength. The rebound in each segment was also very impressive, with a fluctuation of 20 to 30 cents from the lowest point. This was mainly due to the shorts scrambling to cover. In the afternoon, the market became weak again due to reports of a significant earthquake in Japan and a sharp fall in gold prices. However, shorts mostly engaged in closing positions, so trading was very active, with the total volume reaching over 1.8 million bags. Recently, sales in the north have temporarily stopped due to the Japanese invasion, so the near-term outlook is not optimistic. As a result, the September contract fell 7.5 cents from the previous day, the October contract fell 7.5 cents, the November contract fell 1 cent, the December contract fell 7.5 cents, the January contract fell 2.5 cents, and the February contract fell 7.5 cents.

Wheat Futures Market Turns Weak in the Afternoon 85

Yesterday's wheat futures market saw fluctuations in the morning. Although the prices of imported wheat continued to fall, and the gold market saw a sharp decline, most nervous people thought that the Japanese atrocities had occurred and that the source of foreign wheat might be affected. This suspicion caused people's sentiment to rebound, and the opening prices of each segment once jumped by 40 to 50 cents. However, as buyers returned in large numbers, and the sharp fall in gold prices could not be ignored, the prices of each segment gradually declined again. As a result, the closing prices were similar to those of the previous week. In the afternoon, the sentiment that had been strong in the morning turned weak, and the gold market fell sharply again, naturally causing people's sentiment to weaken. Trading in each segment was vigorous, unprecedented in recent times, as both longs and shorts rushed to close positions. Therefore, although the environment was not good, the market did not fall sharply. As a result, the September and October contracts fell 2 cents from the previous weekend, the November and December contracts fell 3 cents, the January contract fell 3 cents, and the February contract fell 2 cents. The spot wheat market saw active trading, with second-grade goods falling to 3.4 taels, and high-quality goods reaching 60 cents. More than 5,000 bags of wheat from Gaoyou, Zhenjiang, Qintong, Yangzhou, and Kunshan were opened.

Silk and Tea: Yixing Autumn Cocoons Not Discounted Much

Drying Discount: 280-290 Catties; Reeling Discount: 430-440 Catties. In recent years, cocoon production in Yixing has become increasingly poor due to the impact of unfavorable weather. This year, most autumn silkworm farmers bred improved varieties. During the major sleep stage, rainwater caused problems. Although cocoon production is only about 40%, the cocoon quality is better. The average drying discount is only 380-390 catties, and the reeling discount is 430-440 catties. The new autumn cocoons are currently being dried and transported to Shanghai one after another.

Foreign Firm Tea Market Turns Quiet 87

Yesterday, the local foreign firm tea market suddenly turned quiet. British and French firms, due to the Japanese invasion of our country, initially caused a sharp rise, but their attitude turned to wait-and-see. Only Gongxi had some transactions in the whole city, and the rest were sparse.

Hardware: English White Iron Sales Smooth

English white iron trading has been very smooth recently because construction groups are enthusiastically purchasing. For example, yesterday, more than 200 dans of No. 31 were opened at a price of 16.75 taels, more than 100 dans of No. 28 were opened at a price of 17 taels, and 70-80 dans each of No. 26 and No. 24 were opened, with No. 26 at 15.75 taels and No. 24 at 14.75 taels. However, investigations show that local inventories are very depleted, so the market is expected to continue to improve.

More Than 2,000 Boxes of American Tinplate Opened 88

Yesterday, tinplate trading suddenly flourished. Investigations show that more than 2,000 boxes were opened throughout the day, with prices at 16 taels for 90 pounds and 17 taels for 100 pounds. It is reported that the openers were from the Xiamen group, and local can factories also completed quite vigorous transactions yesterday.

City Party Headquarters Decides on Anti-Japanese Plan 90

Telegraphing the Central Government to Recover Occupied Territories

Formulating Anti-Japanese National Salvation Work Principles

Passing the Outline of Student Group Organizations

The Municipal Party Headquarters convened a special meeting yesterday to discuss the response to the Japanese military's occupation of Northeast China. The following key issues were resolved:

Important Resolutions: (1) Request the Central Government to promptly recover the occupied territories using revolutionary means, expel the invading Japanese troops, and simultaneously dispatch large forces to defend the coastal ports to strengthen national defense; (2) Telegraph responsible individuals in Guangdong, appealing to them to cease military actions, abolish hostile attitudes, and jointly resist foreign aggression; (3) Telegraph the above two resolutions to all sectors of the country, urging them to advocate them unanimously; (4) Reply to Deputy Commander Zhang; (5) Launch students from all schools to unanimously resist Japan and save the country, with each school separately organizing a student anti-Japanese national salvation association, and charging each school's dean of students with guiding the process; (6) Pass the temporary organizational outline and work principles of the student anti-Japanese national salvation association (attached below); (7) Pass the work principles for the industrial and commercial sectors; (8) Write to the municipal government, urging it to actively organize national defense; (9) Invite leaders from all sectors to talk; (10) Prepare for convening a citywide citizens' meeting.

Work Principles: The work program for national salvation in all sectors should be formulated by each sector itself, but its work must have a scope. The work principles have been decided by the Municipal Party Headquarters and submitted to the Central Government for record. The main points are as follows: (1) Work principles applicable to students: A. Uphold peaceful unification; B. Implement economic severance; C. Strive to promote propaganda; D. Dedicate themselves to academic cultivation; E. Step up military training; F. Avoid all disputes; (2) Work principles applicable to the industrial sector: A, B, C, and F are the same as above, with the addition of one item: Improving work efficiency; (3) Work principles applicable to the commercial sector: also add an item to raise national salvation donations. In addition, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce is urged to supervise merchants to publicly swear to refuse to sell Japanese goods.

Organizational Outline: Each school in this city has an organization of student self-government associations, but their purpose is to create self-governing lives for students within the school. Now that the national crisis is imminent, students from each school will have another organization, specializing in the task of resisting Japan and saving the country. The temporary organizational outline for the student anti-Japanese national salvation association is formulated by the Municipal Party Headquarters as follows: (1) Students of all types of schools above the secondary school level may organize a student anti-Japanese national salvation association; (2) The name of the student anti-Japanese national salvation association must be prefixed with the name of each school; (3) The organization of the student anti-Japanese national salvation association aims to strive to resist Japan and save the country in the spirit of the Three Principles of the People; (4) The work of the student anti-Japanese national salvation association is based on the following principles: A. Uphold peaceful unification; B. Implement economic severance; C. Strive to promote propaganda; D. Dedicate themselves to academic cultivation; E. Step up military training; F. Avoid all disputes; (5) The power of the student anti-Japanese national salvation association belongs to all members, exercised by the members' meeting or the representative meeting; (6) The student anti-Japanese national salvation association establishes a cadre council, with the number of cadres set at five to twenty-one people; (7) Under the cadre council of the student anti-Japanese national salvation association, there are document affairs, propaganda inspection, and other sections, with each section assigned to cadres by mutual election; (8) When necessary, the student anti-Japanese national salvation association may elect one to two representatives to contact the representatives of the anti-Japanese national salvation associations of other schools to hold joint meetings; (9) The charter of the student anti-Japanese national salvation association must comply with the outline system of this association and be submitted to the Shanghai Special City Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang for record; (10) This outline is implemented by the resolution of the Shanghai Special City Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang.

City Party Headquarters' Telegram to the Central Executive Committee 91

Requesting Troop Deployment to Recover Lost Territory

The Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters sent an urgent telegram to the Central Executive Committee yesterday regarding the Japanese military's invasion and occupation of Manchuria. (Omitted salutations) Japanese imperialism has been scheming for a long time to seize the East. This time, taking advantage of our natural disasters and bandit troubles, they suddenly deployed troops, forcefully occupied the East, peered into Pingjin, and attempted to invade Jiaoji, brutally killing our people, burning and looting our homes, capturing our military and civilian leaders, and robbing our barracks and factories. They regard justice as worthless and human life as grass. Their wild nature and atrocities are like madness. Anyone with life and breath can no longer tolerate it. Our national army has compromised in every way, without any resistance. This is not enough to slightly move their pity or restrain their wild ambitions. Our Central Government, with its insight into the overall situation, will certainly take the most appropriate means and the most effective response. Specifically, I silently observe the people's feelings are aroused, righteous indignation is difficult to suppress, and in addition to my sorrow, I dare to offer my humble advice. I hope the Assembly will follow the Prime Minister's teachings, lead the whole people, and devote itself to the revolution, with the sole purpose of seeking China's freedom and equality. But now, the oppression of freedom and inequality imposed on our compatriots by foreign races is even worse than before. Protecting the country and defending the people, defending against aggression, depends solely on the national army. Since our country has suffered such a humiliation, even if we strive for retreat, there must be a limit to retreat. Even if we are willing to be slaughtered, we should choose the method of slaughter. Knowing that the country is declining and collapse is worrying, we have some reluctance, which will disrupt the overall plan. But now, how can this be called a small matter? If this can be tolerated, what cannot be tolerated? Rather than waiting to die with our hands tied, why not fight for survival? Rather than being slowly tortured and wailing, why not cut our throats and commit suicide? As the saying goes, a scholar can be killed, but not humiliated. This is true for individuals, and it is also true for the country. Shall we remain silent and wait for foreign aid? Then the great powers will not help a country that does not express its autonomy. Shall we call out for international justice? Then justice is not set up for a nation that has no courage. Shall we delay the time in preparation for an alliance under the city? Then the Treaty of Shimonoseki in 1895 must first go through the war of 1894. Alas, Serbia is but a small country that has never yielded to the iron hoof of Austria. Turkey is also called a sick man, but it has never yielded to the gunboats of Greece. India is controlled by Britain, but the spirit of resisting Britain is still there. Korea has already fallen to Japan, but the efforts to oppose Japan have not diminished. Today, the whole country, from top to bottom, is truly calm, but how is this different from willingly becoming subjugated people? Tolerance is truly tolerant, but how is this different from being a prisoner awaiting execution? If this continues, all countries will follow suit. Not only will our country no longer become an independent country, but also we will have no face to be people who steal life. Therefore, rather than swallowing our voices and dying, why not take up arms and die for our lives? I urge the Assembly to carefully consider the gains and losses and preside over the overall plan, on the one hand, to urge the Guangdong side to realize the truth and complete the peaceful unification, and on the other hand, to change the policy of non-resistance, resolutely mobilize large forces, and quickly recover the lost territories, deploy heavy troops to protect the ports, even if our territory is again trampled and our people are further slaughtered, it may be that the world and future generations will know that the Chinese people still have this last heroic act. Moreover, how could our sick man of the East never have a Kemal Pasha? And how could our Chinese Kuomintang never reach the young Kuomintang of Turkey? If the Assembly truly makes a decisive decision and issues a nationwide order, all my comrades and compatriots will pledge to support the Central Government, either as a backup or as a vanguard, and will go through fire and water without hesitation, and will not look back on this matter. The telegram is urgent, and I hope you will understand. Chinese Kuomintang Shanghai Special City Executive Committee Horse Seal.

Front-Line Troops Swear to Fight to the Death Without Turning Back

This cannot be resolved through reason and law. It is undeniable that we are poor and weak, but there is no reason to sit idly by and await death. As evidenced by past events, when England invaded Duránce, the entire country was mobilized, yet Duránce still resisted for several years. Similarly, when France and Spain invaded Morocco, the two countries combined their strength, but Morocco also fought back for many years. Both Duránce and Morocco are small, insignificant places. There has never been a case where one can survive by sitting idly by and relying solely on the upholding of justice by onlookers. This principle is very clear. At this critical time of survival, there is absolutely no room for hesitation or procrastination. We should ask the Central Government to resolutely and decisively make preparations for a national mobilization. I, Xinhui, have spent half my life in the military and have a small reputation for battlefield matters. I will charge ahead and fight to the death, with no turning back. This urgent telegram is sent, awaiting your instructions." Lai Xinhui respectfully submits, Ma.

Garrison Command's Preventive Measures 99

Concentrate Police Force to Maintain Order

The Shanghai-Songhu Garrison Command, in accordance with the Central Government's instructions regarding Japan's large-scale invasion of the Eastern Provinces, strictly ordered its subordinate units to remain calm and await a proper resolution. Yesterday, a special notice was issued to the troops stationed along the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou railways, as well as the troops stationed in Shanghai, to comply with the following: (1) Strengthen security within the garrison area and strictly order troops to avoid conflicts with the Japanese; (2) Strictly protect Japanese residents; (3) Sincerely hope that the people will maintain their patriotic fervor with a spirit of perseverance and refrain from acting outside the law, so that the Japanese have no excuse to exploit; (4) Strictly prevent reactionary elements from taking the opportunity to cause trouble.

Double Tenth Festival

Police Contingent Parade Canceled

Strictly Orders Subordinate Units to Remain Calm

Do Not Give Japanese Any Excuse to Exploit

The police contingent under the jurisdiction of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau was originally established to provide extra security and temporary deployment during emergencies to increase police force. It is customary to hold a grand parade once a year. This year, it was scheduled to be held on the Double Tenth National Day. However, due to the Liaoning incident, in order to stabilize public sentiment and consolidate public order, the municipal authorities have ordered the public security bureaus in various districts to redouble their efforts in patrolling and protecting stores and residents of Chinese and foreign nationals. The Public Security Bureau has also assigned various squadrons of the police contingent to the jurisdictions of various district bureaus to jointly undertake patrol and protection work, in order to ensure thoroughness and peace for the people. Therefore, the parade of the police contingent for this year's Double Tenth Festival has been ordered to be canceled so that they can concentrate on their mission.

Beishi Rice Merchants Concerned About the National Crisis 100

Will Not Trade with Japanese Merchants

Will Not Report or Load Japanese Ships

The Beishi Office of the Shanghai Bean and Rice Industry Association convened an emergency meeting of all members yesterday. More than 30 people attended the meeting. Chairman Fu Qian'geng reported that this year's floods have caused disasters, and the rice-producing areas of Jiangsu Province have turned into swamps. Even in the higher areas, the harvest has been reduced. The city's food problem cannot be solved without purchasing foreign rice. However, Japan, taking advantage of our country's severe flood disaster, using the Nakamura incident as an excuse, has dispatched a large army to invade the Northeast, trampling on Shenyang and wantonly ravaging it, regarding our country as meat on the chopping board, with the intention of swallowing it. The members of our industry are members of the nation, and the nation and the family are all closely related. We should rise up and jointly resist foreign aggression. Considering that our industry only purchases foreign rice and does not trade with Japanese merchants or load Japanese ships, there is no other contact with Japanese merchants. In the future, we will boycott Japanese merchants for the foreign rice purchased and the ships loaded by our members. Please discuss and make a public decision, etc. The original proposal was unanimously adopted. In the future, all members must resolutely boycott Japanese merchants for the foreign rice purchased and the ships loaded, and avenge the national humiliation.

Commentary from the Ta Mei Evening News. Yesterday, the Ta Mei Evening News commented on the Japanese military's atrocities in Manchuria, stating briefly: "The Japanese military's occupation of Shenyang overnight, consolidation of its military position throughout Manchuria, disarmament of Chinese troops, concentration of troops on the Korean border, and dispatch of warships to various ports in North China are actions that naturally constitute acts of war. Only the most foolish can believe that they are merely local incidents arising solely from the protection of a section of the railway. Moreover, the claim that the railway was destroyed has not yet been verified. Even as reported, if it was destroyed at 10:30 p.m. on Friday night, it must have been repaired immediately, so there was no disruption to the South Manchuria Railway's schedule. If trains can run as usual, then there must be no disturbance outside the railway area. Therefore, even according to the Japanese report, it is clear that the Japanese military has mobilized its forces based on a theoretical incident to occupy the area. The true reason is that Japan has decided not to resolve the outstanding issues with China through diplomatic negotiations and believes that European and American countries are too preoccupied with their own affairs to criticize its violation of the Open Door Policy, breach of the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and disregard for the Nine-Power Treaty. However, whether Japan's hopes can be fulfilled remains to be seen. In short, the opinions of other countries cannot be ignored. Now, Tokyo's declaration seeks to create the impression that the occupation of Shenyang was the result of overzealous actions by resident military officers and not the intention of the Japanese government's foreign policy. However, for Japan's sake, the only truly effective foreign declaration at present is in deeds, not empty words. The only way is to immediately withdraw the Japanese troops from the newly occupied areas, immediately negotiate compensation for damages in areas outside the railway area, and apologize for actions that exceeded the normal limits of police powers. However, all of this seems unlikely to be done by Japan at this time. If this incident is indeed the result of Japanese militarists acting without government control, then Japan, which usually criticizes China's lack of control over its government troops, is now repeating the same mistake. How weak is its government's power! Japan's insistence on its special status in Manchuria is an old refrain. Its declaration that it does not want third parties to interfere may violate the Nine-Power Treaty to maintain the status quo in Manchuria and the Kellogg-Briand Pact. In the future, even if Europe and America, as Japan expects, do not have time to pay attention to the disputes in the Far East, its victory in Manchuria will ultimately be difficult to achieve as it envisions. Because if Japan seizes any rights in China, it will only further consolidate the position of other countries in the Far East. Those foreigners in China who express sympathy for Japan can take Korea and Taiwan as a warning," and so on.

Anti-Japanese Association

Severely Punish Zhang Bingsheng 104

Robbing Confiscated Japanese Goods

And Committing Violence While Drunk

Xin Sheng News Agency reported that the Anti-Japanese Association of this city has been working very hard in recent days. Inspections are especially strict in the Ning-Shao port area. However, some good merchants, due to the increase in confiscated goods and the loss of capital, do not hesitate to be blinded by profit. Zhang Bingsheng, a shareholder of the Daxin Transportation Company, usually specializes in transporting Japanese goods as his business. A few days ago, he transported more than ten pieces of Japanese goods to the North Station, which were confiscated by the Anti-Japanese Association. Zhang then invited Lu Bingzhang, who claimed to be the head of the defense corps, to lead dozens of hooligans to forcibly rob several pieces. He also threatened that if the goods were confiscated again, he would either beat the inspectors to death or gouge out the eyes of Zhang Gang, the director of the Zhabei inspection department. Yesterday, Zhang again gathered dozens of thugs, first drinking heavily in a restaurant, and then broke into the Anti-Japanese Association, regardless of the situation, beating everyone they encountered. Fortunately, the Anti-Japanese Association's special team received the news and rushed to the scene. The thugs, seeing the situation was not good, fled in all directions. However, Zhang was still not sober and continued to curse and look for people to beat. He was then arrested. The Inspection Section reported the situation to the Standing Committee. At that time, the 17th meeting was being held, and everyone agreed that Zhang Bingsheng dared to lead thugs to attack the Anti-Japanese Association during this tense period of anti-Japanese sentiment and must be severely punished. However, Zhang was still not sober, so they decided to wait until he sobered up before handling the matter.

At the last general meeting, the National Government's Flood Relief Committee decided to allocate 300,000 yuan in relief funds to Jiangsu Province. Under the supervision of Cheng Jingsheng, the Jiangsu Commissioner, the funds were distributed according to the severity of the disaster in various counties of Jiangsu Province as follows: Xinghua, 40,000 yuan; Jiangdu, Gaoyou, Taixian, Baoying, Dongtai, and Yancheng, 30,000 yuan each; Jiangpu, Liuhe, Yixing, and Wujiang, 5,000 yuan each; Liyang, 4,000 yuan; Lishui and Gaochun, 3,000 yuan each. The remaining 40,000 yuan was allocated for running shelters. Another 35,000 bags of flour were allocated. Please review and verify. Zhu Qinglan, September 20.

Jiangsu Flood Relief Association News 106

Funing's floodwaters continue to rise. A telegram was received from the Funing County Relief Branch and Flood Relief Aftermath Branch stating: (Above omitted) After the two telegrams from Hui and Tan, in just a few days, the water level continued to rise by one or two feet due to the concentration of water in the downstream areas. Counting the previous rise, it exceeds one zhang (ten feet). The disaster area has increased to include districts 2, 3, 6, 8, and 12, bringing the total to eleven districts, covering nine-tenths of the entire county. Despite sending teams to hire workers for rescue and setting up shelters in different districts, many still lack assistance, and even those rescued face difficulties in recovery. Apart from requesting Mr. Hao, a philanthropic gentleman, to urgently provide 10,000 yuan for relief, the severity and extent of the disaster, combined with the poverty of the area and the lack of self-help capacity, necessitates sending more personnel with substantial funds to conduct rescues by different routes, so that the people who have suffered a major calamity may feel revived. (Below omitted)

Actual Situation of Disaster in Jiangning: Jiangning County has a total of ten districts. Except for districts 3 and 8, where the disaster situation is slightly less severe, the inundated area in the first district is approximately 94,730 mu (about 15,620 acres); the inundated area in the second district is approximately 4,680 mu (about 770 acres); the inundated area in the fourth district is approximately 124,250 mu (about 20,500 acres); the inundated area in the fifth district is approximately 72,340 mu (about 11,930 acres); the inundated area in the sixth district is approximately 152,840 mu (about 25,240 acres); the inundated area in the seventh district is approximately 32,150 mu (about 5,300 acres); the inundated area in the ninth district is approximately 69,000 mu (about 11,380 acres); and the inundated area in the tenth district is approximately 70,000 mu (about 11,550 acres), accounting for approximately seventy to eighty percent of the entire county's area. As for the embankments and dikes in Jiangning, those inundated include 39 dikes such as Yaohua Dike in the first district, the Zhabei Dike and the Third Dike in the second district, 64 dikes such as Guangyang Dike in the fourth district, 27 dikes such as Changchun Dike in the fifth district, 50 dikes such as Wan'an Dike in the sixth district, 84 dikes such as Yifeng Dike in the seventh district, 131 dikes such as Xiaoyao Dike in the ninth district, and all of the Shazhou Dike in the tenth district. Furthermore, the dikes in the first, ninth, and tenth districts are all located along the Yangtze River, while the dikes in the second, fourth, fifth, sixth, and seventh districts are all located near the banks of the Qinhuai River. Due to the increasing tidal surge, the water could not be discharged, resulting in complete inundation.

Chongming's Request for Relief: A letter was recently received from the Chongming County Relief Branch, stating: (Above omitted) This county is surrounded by the sea. In late last month, strong winds, heavy rain, and high tides occurred simultaneously, causing significant damage to coastal dike projects. More than 90,000 mu (about 14,850 acres) of farmland have been affected, over 1,400 houses have collapsed, and around 100 residents have drowned. A total of over 7,000 people are affected. Those dying of starvation are awaiting relief anxiously. Those who survived the calamity are truly pitiful. It is the duty of this association, and we dare not neglect it. We are currently coordinating with the county's party and government agencies, as well as local legal institutions and schools, to actively raise donations and expedite emergency relief to provide temporary assistance. However, the damage is extensive, the disaster area is vast, and our resources are limited, making comprehensive relief difficult. Therefore, we earnestly appeal to your association to treat everyone equally and quickly extend a helping hand. The gratitude for saving lives will be deeply felt. The urgency of this telegram cannot be overstated. (Below omitted)

Summary of Relief Efforts in Henan by the Jisheng Association 109

The Chinese Jisheng Association, recognizing the extreme suffering caused by both banditry and floods in Nanyang and Tanghe counties, initially allocated funds to the Nanyang branch of the association, led by Chairman Yao Junzhongbang, for emergency relief. Subsequently, based on reports of extensive damage and insufficient funds, the association allocated an additional 5,000 yuan for urgent relief and entrusted it to Chairman Yao of the county branch for distribution. Recently, the association received a report from the chairman of the branch stating that they plan to distribute the funds in Tanghe first, followed by Nanyang. Considering the possibility that autumn crops may not be replanted after the floods in both counties, the association has instructed the branch chairman to conduct a thorough investigation and decide whether to allocate funds for seeds and plan the distribution of winter relief based on the replanting situation. Furthermore, due to the severe disaster in Shenqiu County in eastern Henan, which has suffered from years of banditry and several lost cities, causing the people to be impoverished and displaced, the association is currently facing financial difficulties and can only provide relief to this county. It will strictly and generously distribute aid to alleviate the people's suffering. Previously, the director of the association's relief efforts in Henan, Feng Yangshan, reported that the disaster in Shenqiu was severe, and the association agreed to provide relief to the county, which was deemed crucial. The association had previously raised some funds for emergency relief, but considering the need for seeds to enable replanting and the hope for a good autumn harvest to ensure food for the people this winter and next spring, the association added more funds. Yesterday, the association telegraphed and instructed Director Feng Yangshan to personally inspect the disaster and distribute emergency relief with relief workers, and to plan for seed procurement to prepare for replanting. The association recognizes that the disaster situation in Henan Province is no less severe than in other provinces, and the number of affected counties is among the highest. Before the floods, the province suffered various other calamities, and charitable organizations have not been able to fully address the disaster in Henan. The association hopes that fellow philanthropists will take a unique approach and rescue the suffering people of Henan Province, which is the heartfelt plea of all.
