The Yuan Shunwu Case 111

Three Kidnappers Executed by Firing Squad

Sentenced by the Garrison Headquarters

Executed yesterday by the Municipal Public Security Bureau

In the case of Yuan Shunwu, a student at Great China University, who was kidnapped in front of the school on October 24th last year, the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Sixth District, in conjunction with the Detective Team and the Inspectorate, arrested the kidnappers Fang Dewen and two others. After interrogation and transfer to the Military Law Office of the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, their confessions were found to be truthful, and they were sentenced to death according to the law. The Garrison Headquarters issued the execution order to the Municipal Public Security Bureau on the 21st of this month. The original announcement is recorded as follows: "Announcement No. 65 (Law) of the Songhu Garrison Headquarters: Regarding the announcement, the case of kidnappers Fang Dewen, etc., submitted to the headquarters by the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau has been investigated. The investigation revealed that the criminals Fang Dewen, Yi Peihan, and Xiao Jianxing jointly kidnapped and extorted ransom, providing conclusive evidence. Their crimes are unforgivable and they should be sentenced to death in accordance with Articles 1 and 2 of the Regulations for the Punishment of Kidnappers. The criminals are handed over to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau to verify their identities, bind them, and execute them by firing squad in the execution ground as a deterrent. This is for public notice. Names of the executed criminals: Fang Dewen, age 41, from Taoyuan; Yi Peihan, age 35, from Hubei; Xiao Jianxing, age 28, from Hubei. September 19th, 20th year of the Republic of China, Commander Xiong Shihui."

Sinking of Municipal Ferry No. 5 112

Location: Qingning Temple Wharf

Time: 3:00 AM Yesterday

Municipal Ferry No. 5, operating between Dinghai Bridge and Qingning Temple, sank at Qingning Temple Wharf at around 3:00 AM yesterday. The vessel was insured by the Ning Shao Commercial Steamship Company's insurance department, which was immediately notified and sent personnel to investigate. Efforts are underway to salvage the vessel. The cause of the accident will be determined after the vessel is salvaged. To maintain traffic at the location, the Ferry Management Office has temporarily replaced the sunken vessel with another one.

Discovery of Fake Military Recruitment in Pudong 113

On the 19th of this month, an armed individual wearing a "49th Division of the Army" insignia and resembling a military officer presented himself to District Chief Zhang with a business card printed with the title "Recruiting Officer Wang Licai, Cavalry Training Team and Cavalry First Brigade, General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force." He requested protection for recruitment activities and set up a recruitment station at the home of Guo Desheng, an Anhui native, located at No. 3, Yongji Lane, Huayuan Stone Bridge, Lannidu. A recruitment flag was displayed in the lane, reading "Recruitment Office, 49th Division Headquarters, Recruiting Volunteer Recruits." Unexpectedly, at 3:00 PM yesterday, Chu Zhiwu, a lieutenant attached to the Communications Office of the Engineering Battalion of the 49th Division of the Army, stated that he had discovered someone impersonating the division's name and privately recruiting recruits in Huayuan Stone Bridge, Pudong, and requested immediate detention. After interrogating Wang Licai, District Chief Zhang ordered him to remove his uniform and handed him over to the General Bureau for further investigation that evening, along with a document detailing the case.

Detention for Privately Selling Military Appointment Certificates 114

Private Organization Established in the French Concession

Discovered by the Garrison Headquarters Detectives

Wang Bin, a detective from the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, reported to the French Concession police that someone had established a private organization at No. 38, Ximen Lane, Ximen Road, selling appointment certificates and other items, thereby committing the crime of swindling and deception. He requested detention for further investigation. The police chief ordered detectives to assist in apprehending Zhou Liuwu, seizing numerous pieces of evidence such as appointment certificates and badges, and bringing him into the police station. Yesterday morning, he was handed over to the Criminal Division of the Second Special Court. Fei Xizhen, a lawyer from the police station, explained the case, stating that the police were prosecuting based on Articles 363 and 364 of the Criminal Law for fraud. Wang Bin, a detective from the Garrison Headquarters, stated that the headquarters had recently received reports that someone was impersonating the commander of the Newly Organized Sixth Division, opening rooms in the Great China Hotel and Shenzhou Hotel to sell appointment certificates. The detectives went to apprehend him, but he had already fled. Subsequently, the Garrison Headquarters received a report that the organization was located at No. 38, Ximen Lane, Ximen Road, and they went to arrest Zhou Liuwu, who claimed to be the Major General Counselor of the Sixth Division. Numerous items such as appointment certificates were seized. It was also reported that accomplices had fled to Nanjing, and telegrams have been sent for their arrest. He requested permission for extradition for investigation. Zhou confessed that he was from Fujian and was actually appointed by a Mr. Cheng, the commander of the Newly Organized Sixth Division, as a civilian Major General Counselor, and denied impersonation. The remaining statements were evasive. Judge Luo instructed the defendant to be remanded in custody for further questioning at a later date.

Method for Purchasing Charity Champagne Raffle Tickets in Advance 116

Due to the pressing timeframe for the Chinese Jockey Club's charity champagne raffle, in addition to ordering the printing house to expedite production, the following advance purchase method has been specifically established for the convenience of buyers: Those who come to purchase are allowed to sign up in advance for the number of tickets they want. They can then pick up the tickets upon payment between October 1st and 5th. If they are not picked up during that period, the tickets will not be reserved. For large purchases, buyers can present bank checks to the club to reserve their purchase, and the club will issue a temporary receipt. The original receipt should be kept for ticket exchange at any time.

The Family Scandal of Gao Juchuan 117

Jiang Fuchun's Conduct is Shameful

Gao Juchuan, a detective from the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Detective Team, lived in Changkang Lane, Fangbang Road. At 2:00 PM on August 5th of this year, Gao returned home and saw his wife, Mrs. Gao Chen, gambling at home with a group of young people. Jiang Fuchun was among them, wearing shorts with his buttons undone. Gao found his appearance repulsive and immediately beat Jiang and extorted 100 yuan from him. Later, the Municipal Public Security Bureau sent an inspector to investigate the situation, and Gao was dismissed and transferred to the District Court. After preliminary investigation by Prosecutor Zhao, Gao Juchuan was prosecuted for obstructing freedom, extortion, and dereliction of duty. His wife, Jiang Fuchun, and the gamblers were also prosecuted for gambling. Judge Deng opened the court session yesterday. Gao Juchuan testified, "I returned home and saw my wife on the toilet, while Jiang Fuchun was standing naked in front of the bed. I asked what was going on, and they said they were playing mahjong. I said, 'How can two people play?' Jiang Fuchun's face changed, and I wouldn't let him leave. Later, the people upstairs found out and said he was a neighbor. Then I called the police. The police said it was a trivial matter of little importance. Later, my colleagues came, and I also went out. Later, I reported the adultery to the court. At that time, Jiang Fuchun had written a note." The judge reviewed the note and said, "This note is written to indicate that they cannot gamble. It has nothing to do with adultery." Gao replied, "They can be used interchangeably. Otherwise, why would they write a note for gambling? Every day when I come home, someone says that turtle is back, so they are committing adultery. It is a fact." Wang Aweng testified that he lived at No. 4, Changkang Lane. Gao's wife ordered a maid to invite him to play mahjong. Gao returned and beat Jiang Fuchun, so he fled home. He didn't know what happened after that. Gao Chen testified, "Gao Juchuan is my husband. On August 5th, we didn't succeed in playing because we were short of one player. I was in the room, and Jiang Fuchun also came to my room to play." The judge asked, "What do you mean by 'play'?" She replied, "It was a momentary mistake. I have committed adultery with him three or four times. My husband did not handcuff Jiang, nor did he extort him." Jiang Fuchun testified that he was a traveling salesman for medicinal materials and had no adultery with the woman. He said that he was playing mahjong that day, and when Gao entered, he slapped him, causing his glasses to fall to the ground. As he picked up his glasses, Gao grabbed the handcuffs and handcuffed him, kicking and punching him. He even tried to draw his gun but was stopped. That's why he was extorted for 100 yuan. After questioning the witnesses from both sides, the trial was postponed to another date because the witnesses were not all present.

Completion Ceremony of the New Guangzhao Cemetery 118

Occupying Over 500 Mu

The Guangzhao Cemetery held a completion ceremony at the Dizang Temple Dunzi Hall the other day. Chen Bingqian, representative of the Guangzhao Association, reported: "The old cemetery is full, so the directors of the association purchased over 300 mu of land at the border of the two towns of Jiangwan Dachang to build a new cemetery. I, Bingqian, was appointed as the engineering director. We subsequently purchased over 100 mu, half for a public cemetery to serve as a model, and half for a public burial ground to benefit the poor. We opened roads along the way and built bridges so that vehicles could reach the cemetery directly. We have been working for six years and have spent hundreds of thousands of gold. Today, the new 500-mu cemetery is finally completed, which is gratifying for all our fellow villagers." Guests Wang Binyan and Wu Ziyuan, representative of the Huai'an Hall, and other representatives also delivered speeches. Groups visiting the cemetery included representatives Wang Binyan and Shen Lianfang from the Zhabei Charity Group and the military band, Guo Zhongliang from the Chaozhou Association, Yang Huchen from the Dapu Fellow Villagers Association, Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association, Siming Association, Jiaying Five Districts Fellow Villagers, Chao Hui Association, all of whom sent representatives. The Huai'an Hall, Nanhai Association, Panyu Association, Miscellaneous Grain Merchants Shentang, and Guangbang Teahouse Association all sent congratulatory messages. Police officers from the Fifth District of the Public Security Bureau, the Zhabei Security Regiment, and the Guangzhao Public School Boy Scouts were on site to maintain order. The Zhabei Third Section Fire Brigade sent a fire truck with a full crew to take care of things on site. On the same day, Buddhist lay people from the Buddhist Lay Association and all Taoist priests from Guangbang recited scriptures. A new stage was built, and Beijing opera was performed as a gift. The Jingwu Cantonese Music Department and the Songbai Society played music and dramas. Lion dances were performed by various associations. Plaques were presented by various associations and groups, and gifts were presented by various companies and shops to help entertain the guests. The event ended happily at 6:00 PM.

Establishment of the International Dialect Night School 119

A "International Dialect Night School" has been established at No. 2136, Hongxiang Lane, Xinzha Road, British Concession. It offers English and French classes. The instructors are all renowned Chinese and Western figures, and the facilities are perfect. Classes are held from 7:00 PM to 9:00 PM. The English class has already started, and the French class is scheduled to start on October 1st.

Fine for Fire at Xingyuanchang 120

The apprentice who was burned to death was examined yesterday.

The Xingyuanchang Fried Goods and Candy Store, opened by Zhu Lushi at No. 16, Ximen Road, French Concession, caught fire on the 20th, burning apprentice Zhang Jiliang. The police sent detectives to bring Zhu Lushi, the owner of the store, into the police station for investigation. Yesterday morning, the police reported the situation to Prosecutor Ding Shikui of the Second Special Court, who, along with forensic doctor Wei Ligong and clerk Peng Xu, arrived to examine the body. The court was opened. The police informed the court of the situation. Zhang Gushi, the deceased's mother, stated that her husband had passed away and that this was her only son who had been tragically burned to death. She wished to collect the body herself. Zhu Lushi was brought into court by the detectives. He confessed that the fire started in the kitchen of the pavilion upstairs because the apprentice, the deceased, was cooking and did not clean up the embers. Mr. Ding verified the confession and ruled that Zhang Jiliang had died from being burned. The body was collected by Zhang Gushi. At 3:00 PM, the police transferred Zhu Lushi to the Criminal Division of the Second Special Court. Judge Ma Shounan heard the case. Fei Xizhen, a lawyer from the police station, explained the case, stating: "The defendant's store had fire insurance worth 4,500 taels of silver and was doing well in business. At 1:30 AM on the 20th, the fire was caused because the apprentice was cooking and did not clean up the embers completely. The police are prosecuting under Article 187, Section 2 of the Criminal Law. Please investigate." The defendant, Zhu Lushi, confessed that he was sleeping at 12:00 AM that night. When the fire started, someone knocked on the door and shouted that the kitchen upstairs was on fire because the embers from cooking had not been extinguished. He stated that the store had suffered losses of approximately 3,200 taels of silver. Judge Ma verified the confession and sentenced the defendant to a fine of 100 yuan for the fire, which could be commuted to one day of imprisonment for each yuan.

Fire on Connaught Road 121

A fire broke out suddenly and inexplicably at Hou Zichang's carpentry shop at No. 878, Connaught Road, Hongkou, yesterday at around 5:00 PM. The fire quickly pierced through the roof, and smoke filled the air. A large amount of wood was burned, and four houses were also affected. Fire brigades from various districts rushed to the scene and extinguished the fire after more than an hour.

Bandit Jiang Renyong Sentenced to Five Years 122

Jiang Renyong, a bandit, colluded with Xiao San, who is still at large, and Si Lunzi, who has already been killed, on the 13th of this month. Armed with fake pistols, they robbed Chen Simin of his belongings at the intersection of Wangzhi Road and Beile Road in the French Concession. The detectives arrived and arrested Jiang. Yesterday, he was brought to trial at the Second Special District Court. The police lawyer explained the case, and Jiang admitted to the robbery without hesitation. Lawyer Lin Yingqing provided free defense. Judge Ma sentenced Jiang Renyong to five years of imprisonment for the crime of gang robbery with three or more people and deprived him of public rights for five years. The number of days of detention before the judgment was determined will be commuted at a rate of two days for each day of imprisonment. The fake pistol was confiscated.

Arrest of the Initiator of Obscene Flower Drum Opera, Qian Caisheng 123

The Shanghai County Government found that in various rural areas, every autumn season, there would be a group of idlers who hired performers to sing obscene flower drum opera. The government had previously instructed all public security bureaus to strictly arrest them. It has now been reported that Qian Caisheng, a resident of Qianjiatang Village, Shuangxi Township, Second District of the county, initiated and performed obscene flower drum opera day and night for several days, causing a stir in the neighborhood and attracting mixed crowds of men and women. After learning of this, District Chief Peng consulted with Zhao, the director of the Public Security Bureau of the district, and on the day before yesterday, they secretly dispatched officers to arrest the performers Yang Minzhong and the women Gao Laoda and Gao Laoer, along with the ringleader Qian Caisheng, and brought them to the bureau. Soon, dozens of villagers gathered in front of the bureau, making a ruckus and attempting to snatch them away, and making trouble for the village chief, blaming him for capturing them. Director Zhao of the Public Security Bureau, fearing that an accident would occur, sent the four male and female criminals to the county late that night. After being interrogated by the Public Security Section, they were ordered to be detained pending further investigation.

Private Use of Account Funds Leads to Punishment 124

Han Weiyao Sentenced to Six Months in Prison

Han Weiyao, a Shaoxing native working as a debt collector at the Dahua Hardware Store located at 282 East Broadway Road, recently associated with bad friends, indulging in extravagant prostitution and gambling, and squandering money like dirt. Between April and the 16th of this month, he privately used over 1,190 yuan of the store's funds and fled without a trace. The store owner, Mr. Pan, discovered this and reported it to the Hongkou Police Station. Deputy Detective Zhao Bingkun was dispatched and apprehended Han the day before yesterday at a certain inn at 1175 Tianjin Road, taking him into custody. Yesterday, he was brought before the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. According to the police station's lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, the defendant's relatives were trying to reconcile with the plaintiff and were willing to compensate 500 yuan to settle the matter, but the public prosecution portion must be punished according to the law. Following this, the owner of Dahua Hardware Store, Mr. Pan, stated that although the defendant's family had pleaded for a settlement of 500 yuan, the silver dollars had not yet been received. Questioning the defendant, he directly admitted to the private use of the store's funds. After reviewing the evidence, Judge Xiao Xiefen sentenced Han Weiyao to six months in prison as a warning.

Mischievous Children Specialize in Kidnapping 125

Two Naughty Children Involved in Over Ten Kidnapping Cases

Sold to Other Provinces by the Kidnapping Ring Leader

Western and Chinese detectives from the Huishan Police Station previously arrested the kidnapping gang members Zhu Ating, Wu Zhaogan (both from Ningbo), and their fellow villager Fu Faqing. At 20 Jixiang Lane, Gaochang Temple, Huoche Road in the Chinese district, they further apprehended Fujianese woman Lin Wangshi and Cantonese woman Li Chenshi, and rescued an unnamed four-year-old Ningbo child. The case was handed over to the First Special District Court for investigation. The day before yesterday, the suspect Fu Faqing confessed that there was another woman, Lin Dingshi, who bought children and was hiding at 79 Bansongyuan Road in the Chinese district. Chinese Detective Liu Baoshan and Detective Xie Futang, together with Western detectives, secretly went to the location in cooperation with the Public Security Bureau. Just as they arrived near 79 Bansongyuan Road, they saw Si Gen, the four-year-old son of Zhou Ahe from Wuxi, who had been kidnapped from 96 Taopeng Road, playing nearby. His father immediately recognized him without mistake and took him home. The detectives then entered the house and arrested Lin Dingshi, rescuing a four-year-old boy from Henan named Niu Sheng. Lin Dingshi was temporarily detained by the Public Security Bureau. After finding the Henan boy's father, Wen Zhongqing, who lived at 308 Guoqing Road, Zhabei, they notified him to pick up his child. The Ningbo boy, Si Gen, was also taken home by his family. Yesterday morning, the police station brought the mischievous children Zhu Ating and others, along with the five men and women, to the Third Criminal Court of the Special Court. The police station's lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, presented the case and stated that Lin Dingshi, who was also arrested, was currently detained in the local court and requested that the court issue an official letter for her transfer. Following this, the victims Zhou Ahe and Wen Zhongqing successively described the circumstances of their children's disappearances. Then, Ji A'er from Tongzhou testified that his three-year-old son, Jinfa, disappeared from his doorstep on the 1st of this month at a certain address on Taihe Street, Yangshupu, and that Lin Wangshi had sold him to Fujian. Under questioning, the mischievous child Zhu Ating confessed that the three-year-old child Jinfa and the four-year-old child Si Gen were both lured and kidnapped by him and the defendant Fu Faqing. He claimed that the unnamed four-year-old boy in court was kidnapped by others. Fu Faqing admitted to the crime but claimed that two fugitives took them to Lin Wangshi's house to sell, remaining evasive about the rest. The mischievous child Wu Zhaoyan admitted to helping the kidnappers lure and lead away a total of eight children, all of whom were sold to Cantonese people and transferred to Xiamen. Lin Wangshi admitted to buying the three-year-old boy Jinfa, who had already been sent to Fujian. Li Chenshi stated that the unnamed boy in court was brought by an old woman in her fifties, who said that she had suffered from the Hankou flood and wanted to sell the child for 25 yuan. The police lawyer Qian further stated that no family had yet claimed the unnamed four-year-old Ningbo child. Judge Xiao Xiefen ordered all defendants to be remanded in custody separately for further questioning at a later date.

Examination of Two Gruesomely Murdered Female Corpses 126

The Deceased are Gu Cao Shi and Zhou Lü Shi

Homeowner Zhu Yangshan Rushed Back from Wuxi

Feared That Robbers Killed the Two Women

Court Ordered Police to Strictly Investigate the Murderers

The second floor of the Yichang Electrical Material Store at 196 East Hehuaide Road was rented to Zhu Yangshan. Recently, Zhu was in Wuxi on business, so his aunt-in-law Gu Cao Shi, 28 years old, and the maid Zhou Lü Shi, 38 years old, along with Gu's two-year-old daughter, were temporarily residing there. Unexpectedly, Gu Cao Shi and Zhou Lü Shi were simultaneously assassinated with sharp blades, resulting in their deaths. Later, the daughter frantically tapped on the glass window, which was noticed by Zhang Zhijun, a worker at the rice store across the street. He informed the nearby Chinese constables at 1415, who arrived and inspected the scene. They found the two women lying dead in bed, covered in blood, in a very gruesome state. They then notified the Huishan Police Station by phone, ordering detectives to investigate. The bodies of the two women were transported to the Féron Road morgue. Yesterday morning, Inspector Guo Wei from the First Special District Court arrived to examine the bodies and conduct an official inquiry. According to Zhu Yangshan's complaint, he was in Wuxi at the time of the incident, and the house was occupied by his aunt-in-law Gu Cao Shi, whose husband was in Hankou and with whom she did not have a good relationship. The maid Zhou Lü Shi had only been employed for five or six months. He suspected that the simultaneous murder of the two was the work of robbers, as the boxes in his house had all been pried open. Witness Zhang Zhijun also testified to the previous situation. Judge Guo then ordered that since the deceased Gu Cao Shi and Zhou Lü Shi were both killed by knife wounds while alive, Gu Cao Shi's body should be handed over to Zhu Yangshan for coffining and burial, and Zhou Lü Shi's body should be handed over to her brother Lü Rushan for coffining and burial. The police were ordered to strictly investigate the murderers and bring them to justice for questioning.

Page 16

Reader Correspondence

Miss So-and-So Asks (Regarding Negotiating the Dissolution of a Marriage Engagement) 135

I am now twenty-six years old. My parents only arranged my engagement last year to a fifteen-year-old boy. At the time, because of the age difference of more than ten years, I proposed that I did not approve. However, my family is an old-fashioned family, so my parents used autocratic means to arrange the engagement. Now they are pressuring me to marry him. Because I feel that a small child cannot be a lifelong companion, I want to break the engagement, but I am bound by various family constraints and cannot fulfill my wishes. I request guidance and a reply in your newspaper.

(Reply) According to Article 975 of the current Civil Code, "A marriage engagement cannot be forcibly enforced." If you truly do not wish to marry because of the age difference, legally, no one should force you. Also, Article 972 states, "A marriage engagement should be made by the parties themselves." If you did not express your consent at the time, then it is of course possible to dissolve the engagement. However, you should sincerely and gently explain your difficulties to your parents, aiming to achieve your goal without hurting their feelings.

Mr. Li Asks (Please Promote Awareness of the Evils of Gambling) 136

Yesterday, I read a news item in your newspaper's local news section entitled "Féron Vautel Resolves to Ban Chinese and Foreign Gambling Dens," which gave me mixed feelings of joy and sorrow. Sorrow because of Féron Vautel's effort to eliminate harm for the people, and joy because everyone can live and work in peace and take the path of light from now on. Gambling is the most harmful thing, as everyone knows. At worst, it wastes time and causes unemployment; at worst, it leads to bankruptcy and even suicide, as newspapers often report. The psychology of gamblers is mostly based on the hope of getting lucky in order to make a large profit. How can they know that things will go against their wishes, resulting in empty-handedness, loss of morale, and returning empty-handed? I am an example of this. Speaking of it, I am self-reproaching and ashamed. Although I know there is more bad luck than good luck, I am eager to go. If there were no gambling dens, then everyone would live and work in peace and would never have such extravagant thoughts. In recent years, there have been no fewer than ten of the most prominent gambling dens in the French Concession of Shanghai. If they are not closed down soon, what unimaginable consequences will there be? I pity and hate myself, and I especially feel heartbroken when I see others suffering from the same disease. I appeal with no way to be heard, only sighing in vain. Your newspaper has the most credibility and consistently advocates justice and fairness in its special commentary. Could you please make written propaganda on the issue of "gambling" to remind my countless suffering compatriots? This kindness and virtue are a hundred times better than saving disaster victims. I implore the reporter to appreciate my foolish sincerity and publicize this in your newspaper.

(Reply) Your letter is very sincere. You have awakened early and stopped at the brink, which is worthy of respect. You are even more willing to share your experiences with the victims, which makes us even more moved. We respectfully reply to your letter in public to acknowledge your kind intentions. As for this newspaper's prohibition of gambling propaganda, it is the duty of the news media, and we will do our best.

Central Bank Inspection Report 140

Number 102

The 102nd Inspection Report of the Central Bank's Issuance Reserve states: According to Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, this committee is responsible for inspecting the gold and silver reserve for the issuance of convertible banknotes by this bank. The 102nd inspection was conducted on September 19, 1931, at the Issuance Bureau of this bank, and the results of the inspection are announced as follows: (A) Total amount of convertible banknotes issued: 41,267,483 silver dollars, including 38,382,613 silver dollar notes and 2,884,870 yuan for converted currency. Total amount of convertible banknote reserve: 41,267,483 yuan, including cash reserve of 27,661,771 yuan. This cash reserve consists of 18,576,993.61 yuan stored in the bank's issuing vault, 4,045,763 yuan stored in branches in various ports, and 5,039,014.39 yuan deposited with other banks. Guarantee reserve, equivalent to 13,600,5712 silver dollars. (B) Total amount of customs gold unit convertible banknotes issued: 1,000,000 yuan. Total amount of customs gold unit convertible banknote reserve: 1,000,000 yuan. This reserve includes 400,000 US dollars deposited with local banks, at a fixed price of 40 customs gold units to the dollar, as above. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's Convertible Banknote Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is in accordance with the regulations. This report is submitted. September 19, 1931, Li Fusun, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Supervisors Wang Jingli, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Zhiqing, Lin Kanghou, and Xu Ji.

Record of Meeting of Two Medical Associations 141

The National Medical Association held its 12th Executive Committee meeting yesterday, chaired by Xu Naili. The following was discussed: Item 1: The date of the second representative conference, originally tentatively scheduled for mid-November, is now too close, and the floods in various provinces are extremely severe, transportation is inconvenient, and the Japanese invasion is increasing, so fewer representatives from far away will attend. Item 2: The resolution on the preparations for the conference was (1) to notify all members to recommend two attending representatives (2) to recommend Sun Pingjie to be in charge of the exhibition group for the conference, but to refuse to display Japanese goods, etc. Item 3: On how to express the association's opinion on the Japanese invasion, the resolution was to notify the members of the national branches to boycott Japanese medical supplies and to recommend Wang Qizhang and Xia Shenchu to draft a declaration and methods for replacing Japanese drugs to notify all physicians nationwide to be consistent. Item 4: The resolution on the letter from the Jingsha Medical Association of the Chinese Medical Association regarding the second attending representative was approved. Item 5: The resolution on the letter from the Yin County Medical Association requesting the association to request the Ministry of Finance to exempt physicians from advertising donations was that the advertising donation is different from the business tax and there is no need to discuss it. Item 6: The resolution on the letter from Zheng Xinjian of Hefei, Anhui, requesting individual permission to participate in the conference was to participate as an observer.

The Shanghai Medical Association held its 12th Executive Committee meeting of the 5th session yesterday, chaired by Song Guobin. The following was discussed: (1) On how the association should express its opinion on the Japanese invasion of the Eastern Provinces, the resolution was (A) to issue a declaration to stop the civil war and unite against foreign aggression (B) to notify all members not to use Japanese medicines and to have economic severance with Japan (2) Members have already pledged to donate more than 2,000 yuan for disaster relief donations to various provinces, and the resolution was to continue fundraising (3) The resolution was that Shanghai Civilian Maternity Hospital and Hui Sheng Maternity Hospital, Civilian Hospital, and others have successively sent letters expressing their willingness to provide free shelter for disaster-stricken pregnant women to notify the Shanghai Municipal Government Disaster Relief Association to notify all disaster victims. In addition, the diagnosis hospitals of all members of this association will also uniformly waive medical fees for disaster victims to treat diseases, but must uniformly have a certificate from the shelter (4) Song Guobin, Xu Naili, Li Shenwei, You Pengxi, Xia Shenchu, Zhu Qiluo, and Chen Rongzhang were hired by the Shanghai Fundraising Association for Immediate Relief to Various Provinces to serve as executive committee members of the association and concurrently as members of the medical group. The resolution was to retroactively recognize them as attending representatives of the association (5) The resolution on the reply from member Zhu Huoliang was to transfer it to the Supervisory Committee for handling (6) The resolution on the letter from citizen Chen Hongkui seeking public judgment on an injury case was that the section on using the steaming bone method for examination is not scientifically based and there is no way to make a public judgment (7) The resolution on the publication of the association's yearbook was to proceed as planned. The forms that have not been submitted to the members should be submitted to the association by the end of September, and the publication should be completed within one month (8) The applications from physicians Liu Qijing, Zhang Yuxi, Jiang Benyi, She Zhen, Li Anbang, and Gong Hanmei to join the association were resolved.

The itinerary is scheduled for the 25th of this month, taking the 7:00 AM train to Hangzhou, touring the West Lake in the afternoon, and the next morning taking a car to the riverside and taking a small boat to trace the Fuchun River, arriving at Tonglu in the morning, touring the Qili Long in the afternoon, returning by boat at 6:00 PM, arriving in Hangzhou at midnight. That evening coincides with the Mid-Autumn Festival. On the 27th, take a car directly to Haining to watch the midday tide. If the night train is inconvenient, return to Hangzhou; otherwise, wait to see the night tide before returning. On the 28th, take the 5:35 PM train back to Shanghai. The travel fee is twenty-two yuan per person, regardless of gender. Students receive a 10% discount, and children under twelve are half price. It is heard that there are still vacancies. Those who wish to join can contact the YMCA's business department.

Recent News about Ye Xinan's Dictionary 150

Mr. Ye Xinan, the inventor of the Four-Corner Check Character Method, has now begun editing a dictionary. Mr. Ye believes that current dictionaries are not only inconvenient to check, but also that the annotations are mostly in classical Chinese, sometimes the wording is too high and impractical, sometimes the wording is unclear and incomprehensible, or even plagiarized from old dictionaries. Furthermore, they do not take into account the layout, font size, paper brightness, etc., which is not a fundamental way to improve the dictionary. Therefore, in addition to arranging the character positions, Mr. Ye has recently devoted himself to the study of annotation and printing. Soon, he will conduct experiments on the results of his research in Beijing, Shanghai, and other places, and invite educational experts to correct them.

Social News

The Development of Modern Chicken Farming 155

Zhuang Ruiqing

In modern times, chicken farming has become a scientific undertaking, with astonishing advancements and inventions. This is because modern chicken farming is no longer a small-scale side business, but has become a large organization with deliberate planning. There are specific rules and regulations in the management and raising of chickens. Even the equipment in the chicken coops has been greatly renovated, with novel productions and creations. As for the prevention and treatment of chicken diseases, incubation procedures, breeding, mating, and registration, there is even more advanced knowledge and research. Therefore, this kind of scientific chicken farming is truly "hearing what predecessors have never heard."

We must realize that there is an important reason for the development of chicken farming: the method of breeding chickens used to be natural incubation (hen incubation), but now it has advanced to the ingenious artificial incubation method (i.e., machine incubation). We can regard this invention as the driving force for the development of the chicken farming industry, and also as the scientific revolution of the chicken farming industry, which has fundamentally improved and invented all the backward chicken farming methods of the past.

The invention of artificial incubation dates back to 1540 AD, when the Frenchman FrancigI first created an automatic incubator. Later, it was gradually improved, leading to the invention of the current hot water and hot air incubators. The image above shows the latest coal-fired incubator (Jamesway) from Jamesway in the United States, which can incubate two to three thousand eggs at a time. The highest number of eggs that can be incubated by an incubator is reported to be more than 600,000 eggs at a time by the coal-fired hot water incubator made by BuckeyeCo in the United States. The automatic incubator made by Deyuan in Jiangwan, Shanghai, China, can also incubate three to four hundred and eighty eggs at a time. According to our experience, chicks hatched by machine are indeed no inferior to those hatched by natural incubation. Compared with the advantages of both methods, chicks hatched by artificial incubation, as long as they are properly raised, are often stronger than those hatched by natural incubation. Therefore, after the invention of artificial incubation, it not only promoted the development of the chicken farming industry, but also eliminated natural incubation, replacing it with failure (chicks hatched by artificial incubation are raised with artificial brooders).

Although we have a general understanding of the invention and progress of artificial incubation, we should still understand the benefits of chicken farming in order to awaken people's attention and hope that our compatriots will work together to develop the chicken farming industry, increase production, and reduce the pain of unemployment or desperation. Furthermore, if the chicken farming industry can be expanded to the point of "ruralization" in the future, the current danger of the collapse of the rural economy in China may be considerably remedied by the increase in chicken production. Therefore, we should not only regard chicken farming as a "productive undertaking of the times," but also call it a "savior of life panic" or a "relief for the poor and desperate."

If we want to understand the benefits of chicken farming, we must first know the division of chicken farming in the current business world. The current business lines of the chicken farming industry can be roughly divided into three types: (1) breeding chickens, (2) egg-laying chickens, and (3) meat chickens. The standard for managing breeding chickens is determined by the egg-laying record of the breeding chickens raised. For example, in the United States, the famous farms that raise Leghorn breeding chickens include Holywood and Honson. However, the price of each Holywood breeding chicken is usually around US$500 (approximately 2,000 Chinese dollars), while Honson's are only a few tens of US dollars (approximately 200 Chinese dollars). This is because the egg-laying record of Holywood chickens is higher than that of Honson (each Holywood chicken lays about 330 eggs per year, while Honson only lays 300). Therefore, the benefit of managing breeding chickens depends on whether they can improve the high-yield chicken breeds. In other words, if you have advanced knowledge and experience and can create a high-yield breeding chicken (or various standard chickens), then you can gain several times the profit due to social trust.

(2) Egg-laying chickens. Most people who manage this type of chicken farming raise Leghorn chickens, because Leghorn has become a world-famous egg-laying chicken, laying at least about 150 eggs per year. For example, Deyuan's chickens have reached an average of 200. Therefore, the profit from each chicken laying eggs per year in Deyuan is about two yuan (Deyuan's egg-laying chickens cost about 3.6 yuan for feed per chicken per year due to better feed, and each egg is worth 5 cents, which is about 10 yuan for 200 eggs. In addition to labor costs, there is a profit of 2 yuan).

(3) Meat chickens. People who raise meat chickens mostly raise large-breed chickens such as Brahma, Cochin, or Chinese large-breed chickens, because these chickens have strong bodies and tender muscles. People are happy to buy them for sale. The feed cost of Brahma chickens from small to fattening period (fattening terminology) is only about 1.4 yuan, and the meat weight is about 9 to 12 pounds, so the profit is obviously more than double.

Since we have understood the benefits of chicken farming, I sincerely hope that our compatriots across the country will work together to develop chicken farming and increase production to relieve the personal panic of life. Now, I would like to state my personal opinions on the development of the chicken farming industry for the reference of our countrymen.

I am now planning a considerable amount of capital to return to Sichuan to open a chicken farm in Chongqing, and the purpose is to improve the chicken breeds in Sichuan and promote the development of the chicken farming industry. I plan to improve the chicken breeds in two steps: (1) Chick egg exchange method, that is, after the chicken farm develops, hatch a number of chicks with a large incubator every year, and ask the villagers to bring five to ten Chinese chicken eggs to exchange for a Leghorn chick. If so, the villagers will definitely be happy to exchange, and the Leghorn species will naturally be able to spread quickly. (2) Scattered raising and profit collection method, that is, distribute a number of chicks to farmers every year, without charging for the chicks, but only ask them to return ten to fifteen chicken eggs per year for consumption and sale to return the cost.

What we should pay attention to here is that I absolutely do not advocate "hybrid improvement" of the Leghorn species with Chinese chickens. Therefore, the eggs returned by the villagers, regardless of whether they are purebred eggs or not, cannot be used for hatching and promotion because their feeding and breeding are not completely legal. They can only be used as eggs for sale. The success of chicken improvement requires decades of our efforts and dedicated breeding to succeed. The Leghorn chicken has been improved for several generations and has become a standard egg-laying chicken. We should raise this "purebred" chicken as the unit chicken species for improving Chinese chicken breeds, and there is no need to follow the "hybrid improvement" thinking advocated by the general public. The above-mentioned opinions are my suggestions for promoting the improvement of chicken breeds. I hope that the government can help in the future, so that the Chinese chicken breeds can be easily improved in a unified manner in a few years.

A Century Later

The World's Population Will Suffer from Hunger 156

Insufficient Food Production

London News: Professor Thomson of Natural History and Sociologist Gattes have co-authored the book "Life, Outline of General Biology". The book discusses the future trend of world population and food. It states that the total world population is currently 1,750 trillion, with an average annual increase rate of about 12 trillion. The demographer Malthus calculated the world population at 850 trillion during the French Revolution. Compared with the current number, the world population has doubled within a century. In addition, the world's arable land is estimated to be 13,000 trillion acres. Each person needs an average of at least two and a half acres to supply their food. According to the current production and consumption status, the population that can be supported is at most several thousand two hundred trillion, and it is estimated that the population of five thousand two hundred trillion will be reached in another century. If this continues, the world's population will face the danger of food shortage.

Between London and India

Air Transport of Parcels 157

5,000 Miles in 5 Days

London News: The air route between London and Karachi, India (5,000 miles) has been open for three years, but it has only carried passengers, cargo, and letters. Recently, it has begun to load parcels and mail. Water transportation between London and India takes 21 days, but now by air, it only takes 5 days.

The Defeat of Rubber and Tin Market by Qiu Bincun 159

Recently, due to the economic panic in the world, a huge recession has occurred in Nanyang, the supply area of rubber and tin raw materials. At present, the international market price of rubber is still only 13 or 14 yuan per picul, and the market price of tin ore is still only 40 yuan per picul. The revival of the value of rubber and tin is still in a long night, and it is unknown when a glimmer of light can be realized. The method of seeking relief is the most urgent task at present. Therefore, I have written this article on the defeat of the rubber and tin market and the relief of unemployed overseas Chinese to discuss it again and again with those who are concerned about overseas Chinese affairs in Nanyang.

(1) Reasons for the Defeat of the Rubber and Tin Market

Before talking about the defeat of the rubber and tin market, we should first talk about the reasons for its defeat. The reason for the defeat of the rubber and tin market is due to overproduction.

For example, the total amount of rubber produced in various parts of British Malaya in September of last year and the total amount of imports and exports, the output of rubber plantations above 100 acres was 22.172 tons, the output of rubber plantations below 100 acres was 17.772 tons, totaling 39.944 tons, imported 6.67 from foreign countries

Page 20

8 tons, imported 15.282 tons from the Malay States, exported 49.982 tons to foreign countries, and 15.28 tons to local areas. The table is now listed below.

Other rubber producing areas such as the Dutch East Indies, etc., the statistics are not available to me, otherwise there will be amazing numbers. Therefore, Reuters telegraphed that "the stock of rubber in London and Liverpool in early October has increased by 841 tons, and the previous stock is enough to supply the world for seven months." Overproduction can be said to be very huge.

The supply of tin, such as Malaya, Bolivia, Dutch East Indies, Nigeria, etc., the produced tin ore, like rubber, is also trapped in the fate of oversupply. I will not describe it in detail here.

(2) The Impact of the Defeat of the Rubber and Tin Market

The defeat of the rubber and tin market directly caused the bankruptcy of overseas Chinese rubber and tin owners, exporters, and speculators, such as Qicheng Company in Singapore, Wanlixing Company in Penang, Zhicheng Company in Jiangsha, etc., hundreds of millions of capital of merchants went bankrupt one after another, which is its example. The defeat of the rubber and tin market indirectly caused Chinese workers to lose their jobs and have no place to live and support themselves. As reported by the Star News, the recession of rubber and tin has besieged Nanyang. Chinese workers who have nowhere to go went to the consulate to petition, saying that on November 4, about seven or eighty unemployed Chinese workers gathered in front of the consulate. Because they have been unemployed for a long time, they are afraid that waiting here for a long time will make them even more depressed. Therefore, they jointly met with the consul to request repatriation. They had gone to the Protectorate to request, but were not accepted. Then they elected two representatives to meet with the consul. It was heard that Chen Consul believed that it would be good to repatriate these unemployed overseas Chinese. Later, Chen Consul told the representatives that he had visited the President of the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce and various Chinese shipping companies to discuss a proper solution. They all said that it is now the time of falling rubber and tin prices, and the repatriation of unemployed overseas Chinese is more difficult. However, being stranded in a foreign land is a tragedy, and those with a little conscience cannot bear to sit idly by. Moreover, this matter is also related to the national system. The local government originally had a move to repatriate unemployed Chinese workers, but those who were sent were the old, weak, disabled, and sick. Now, many strong overseas Chinese have also embarked on the path of unemployment, which is very pitiful. As for the method of finding repatriation, it is not easy to raise a proper solution suddenly. Moreover, this matter cannot be handled without sufficient financial resources. Therefore, it is now planned that the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce will convene a meeting of fellow Chinese to raise a proper solution. You should also understand that there are countless unemployed Chinese workers now. If everyone wants to be repatriated, it is also a difficult task. It is hoped that they will not lightly say that they will return home unless it is absolutely necessary. Repatriating unemployed overseas Chinese is our responsibility. Repatriation by the local government is a last resort. It is better if our fellow Chinese can send them back themselves. Moreover, the repatriation fee for each person is no more than ten yuan. If the fellow Chinese can work together to deal with this matter, it is not absolutely impossible. However, this matter should also be discussed with the local government, which is more appropriate. Because the repatriation has always been handled by the government, there are already more than 100 unemployed people gathering in the long gallery of the Chinese Affairs Department every night. The hardship of life can be imagined. The Protectorate repatriates old and weak overseas Chinese and unemployed overseas workers every week, and the number often reaches hundreds or even one or two hundred people. However, most of those who are accommodated and repatriated by the Protectorate are old and weak people, or illegal hooligans with disruptive nature. Those who still have the ability to work here are not easily accommodated. Dozens of people who jointly petitioned the consulate did stay in the long pavilion of the Protectorate every night, waiting for the boat to disembark, and because they did not catch up with the Dali Hua ship, these people left the Protectorate and agreed to turn to the consulate for help. Therefore, when they went to the consulate that day, some of them carried rattan boxes or packages and other luggage.

Also, the Penang News reported that the wave of unemployment has poured into Penang, saying that in Penang, the number of unemployed people has been increasing day by day. The local government is urgently thinking of ways to solve the problem in order to appease the people. The Chinese Affairs Department specially convened local people to discuss the issue of unemployment. Those who attended were very enthusiastic. Mr. Mi Dubu proposed that there is no other way to provide relief than to raise funds for relief. He advocated that fundraising should be carried out immediately. He said that Chinese enthusiast Qiu Shanyou has enthusiastically pledged to donate the food expenses of the unemployed shelter for one month, which has already been initiated by someone. It seems that this will be very easy to carry out. After discussion, it was resolved to hold an unemployment registration immediately. All unemployed people can go to the Chinese Assembly Hall to report their current situation in order to investigate how many unemployed people there are, so that it is easy to start relief. When the meeting was held, a group of unemployed people gathered outside the door and elected representatives to enter the meeting place to inquire about the current relief and how to start it. The chairman replied that it could only be decided after discussion. They then dispersed and continued the meeting. Mr. Lin Chengluo proposed that the government should reduce property taxes. He wrote to the Chinese Affairs Department proposing to hold an unemployment registration immediately, and that the current employees should donate one day's salary or wages to help unemployed employees. The Municipal Council should also cooperate as much as possible, as should the landlords, so that all land rents can be reduced. In addition, an agricultural policy should be implemented to allow unemployed workers to engage in agriculture (to be continued).
